I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
feat(pancake): comment auto-reply + first-inbox DM
## Problem Statement
Pancake (pages.fm) channel only processed INBOX webhook events. COMMENT events (from post comments on Facebook, Instagram, etc.) were silently dropped, preventing AI agents from replying to comments or sending first-inbox DMs to commenters.

## Proposal
Extend the Pancake channel to route COMMENT events through the agent pipeline, reply via `reply_comment` action, and optionally send a one-time DM to the commenter via `private_reply` (first-inbox).

## How It Works

- COMMENT webhooks now routed via `switch convType { case "COMMENT": handleCommentEvent() }`
- Feature gate: `features.comment_reply: true` required
- Keyword/all filter: `comment_reply_options.filter: "keyword"` with `keywords: [...]`
- Post context enrichment: optional `include_post_context: true` prepends post text
- First-inbox DM: `features.first_inbox: true` — one-time `private_reply` per sender
- `PostFetcher` with `singleflight` + TTL cache prevents API stampedes

### Architecture
```
Webhook POST (COMMENT event)
  --> webhookRouter.ServeHTTP()
  --> switch convType: INBOX|COMMENT
  --> handleCommentEvent()
       |-> feature gate, self-reply, dedup, filter
       |-> buildCommentContent() [+ optional post context]
       |-> HandleMessage() --> agent pipeline

Send(msg) with pancake_mode="comment"
  --> ReplyComment() [action: reply_comment]
  --> if first_inbox: sendFirstInbox() [action: private_reply]
```

## Challenges
- Pancake requires list-all-posts vs Facebook's per-post Graph API — singleflight key is "posts" not per-postID
- First-inbox dedup is in-memory (resets on restart) — acceptable, re-sending once is benign
- Echo dedup must fire before content enrichment to avoid prefix mismatch

## Plan & Phases
- [x] Phase 1: Types + API Client
- [x] Phase 2: Post Fetcher
- [x] Phase 3: Comment Handler
- [x] Phase 4: Webhook Router + Send Path
- [x] Phase 5: Integration Verification

## Human Review Tasks
- [ ] Verify `reply_comment` and `private_reply` action names match live Pancake API contract
- [ ] Test with a real Pancake page + COMMENT webhook
- [ ] Validate first-inbox DM is delivered only once per commenter

</pr_description>

     1	// Package pancake implements the Pancake (pages.fm) channel for GoClaw.
     2	// Pancake acts as a unified proxy for Facebook, Zalo OA, Instagram, TikTok, WhatsApp, Line.
     3	// A single Pancake API key gives access to all connected platforms — no per-platform OAuth needed.
     4	package pancake
     5	
     6	import "encoding/json"
     7	
     8	// pancakeCreds holds encrypted credentials stored in channel_instances.credentials.
     9	type pancakeCreds struct {
    10	        APIKey          string `json:"api_key"`                  // User-level Pancake API key
    11	        PageAccessToken string `json:"page_access_token"`        // Page-level token for all page APIs
    12	        WebhookSecret   string `json:"webhook_secret,omitempty"` // Optional HMAC-SHA256 verification
    13	}
    14	
    15	// pancakeInstanceConfig holds non-secret config from channel_instances.config JSONB.
    16	type pancakeInstanceConfig struct {
    17	        PageID   string `json:"page_id"`
    18	        Platform string `json:"platform,omitempty"` // auto-detected at Start(): facebook/zalo/instagram/tiktok/whatsapp/line
    19	        Features struct {
    20	                InboxReply   bool `json:"inbox_reply"`
    21	                CommentReply bool `json:"comment_reply"`
    22	        } `json:"features"`
    23	        AllowFrom  []string `json:"allow_from,omitempty"`
    24	        BlockReply *bool    `json:"block_reply,omitempty"` // override gateway block_reply (nil = inherit)
    25	}
    26	
    27	// --- Webhook payload types ---
    28	// These types match the actual Pancake (pages.fm) webhook delivery format.
    29	// Top-level envelope has optional "event_type" + nested "data" containing
    30	// "conversation" and "message" objects.
    31	
    32	// WebhookEvent is the top-level Pancake webhook delivery envelope.
    33	type WebhookEvent struct {
    34	        EventType string          `json:"event_type,omitempty"` // "messaging", may be empty
    35	        PageID    string          `json:"page_id,omitempty"`    // top-level page_id (some formats)
    36	        Data      json.RawMessage `json:"data"`
    37	}
    38	
    39	// WebhookData is the "data" envelope inside a Pancake webhook event.
    40	type WebhookData struct {
    41	        Conversation WebhookConversation `json:"conversation"`
    42	        Message      WebhookMessage      `json:"message"`
    43	        PageID       string              `json:"page_id,omitempty"` // page_id may appear here or top-level
    44	}
    45	
    46	// WebhookConversation holds the conversation metadata from a Pancake webhook.
    47	type WebhookConversation struct {
    48	        ID          string        `json:"id"`                    // format: "pageID_senderID"
    49	        Type        string        `json:"type"`                  // "INBOX" or "COMMENT"
    50	        AssigneeIDs []string      `json:"assignee_ids,omitempty"` // Pancake staff IDs assigned to this conversation
    51	        From        WebhookSender `json:"from"`
    52	        Snippet     string        `json:"snippet,omitempty"`
    53	}
    54	
    55	// WebhookSender identifies the message sender.
    56	type WebhookSender struct {
    57	        ID             string `json:"id"`
    58	        Name           string `json:"name"`
    59	        Email          string `json:"email,omitempty"`
    60	        PageCustomerID string `json:"page_customer_id,omitempty"`
    61	}
    62	
    63	// WebhookMessage holds the message payload from a Pancake webhook.
    64	type WebhookMessage struct {
    65	        ID              string              `json:"id"`
    66	        Message         string              `json:"message,omitempty"`          // primary text content
    67	        OriginalMessage string              `json:"original_message,omitempty"` // unformatted fallback
    68	        Content         string              `json:"content,omitempty"`          // legacy field
    69	        From            *WebhookSender      `json:"from,omitempty"`             // actual sender of this message
    70	        Attachments     []MessageAttachment `json:"attachments,omitempty"`
    71	        CreatedAt       json.Number         `json:"created_at,omitempty"`
    72	}
    73	
    74	// MessageAttachment represents a media attachment in a Pancake webhook message.
    75	type MessageAttachment struct {
    76	        Type string `json:"type"` // "image", "video", "file"
    77	        URL  string `json:"url"`
    78	}
    79	
    80	// MessagingData is the normalized internal representation used after parsing.
    81	type MessagingData struct {
    82	        PageID         string
    83	        ConversationID string
    84	        Type           string // "INBOX" or "COMMENT"
    85	        Platform       string // "facebook", "zalo", "instagram", "tiktok", "whatsapp", "line"
    86	        AssigneeIDs    []string
    87	        Message        MessagingMessage
    88	}
    89	
    90	// MessagingMessage is the normalized message used by the handler.
    91	type MessagingMessage struct {
    92	        ID          string
    93	        Content     string
    94	        SenderID    string
    95	        SenderName  string
    96	        Attachments []MessageAttachment
    97	}

   104	        Name     string `json:"name"`
   105	        Platform string `json:"platform"` // facebook/zalo/instagram/tiktok/whatsapp/line
   106	        Avatar   string `json:"avatar,omitempty"`
   107	}

   112	        Message    string   `json:"message,omitempty"`
   113	        ContentIDs []string `json:"content_ids,omitempty"`
   114	}

   119	        URL string `json:"url,omitempty"`
   120	}

     1	package pancake
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"
     5	        "encoding/json"
     6	        "fmt"
     7	        "log/slog"
     8	        "net/http"
     9	        "sync"
    10	        "time"
    11	
    12	        "github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/bus"
    13	        "github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/channels"
    14	        "github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/store"
    15	)
    16	
    17	// Compile-time interface assertions.
    18	var (
    19	        _ channels.Channel           = (*Channel)(nil)
    20	        _ channels.WebhookChannel    = (*Channel)(nil)
    21	        _ channels.BlockReplyChannel = (*Channel)(nil)
    22	)
    23	
    24	const (
    25	        dedupTTL        = 24 * time.Hour
    26	        dedupCleanEvery = 5 * time.Minute
    27	        outboundEchoTTL = 45 * time.Second
    28	)
    29	
    30	// Channel implements channels.Channel and channels.WebhookChannel for Pancake (pages.fm).
    31	// One channel instance = one Pancake page, which may serve multiple platforms (FB, Zalo, IG, etc.)
    32	type Channel struct {
    33	        *channels.BaseChannel
    34	        config        pancakeInstanceConfig
    35	        apiClient     *APIClient
    36	        pageID        string
    37	        pageName      string // resolved from Pancake page metadata at Start()
    38	        platform      string // resolved from Pancake page metadata at Start()
    39	        webhookSecret string // optional HMAC-SHA256 secret for webhook verification
    40	
    41	        // dedup prevents processing duplicate webhook deliveries.
    42	        dedup sync.Map // eventKey(string) → time.Time
    43	
    44	        // recentOutbound suppresses short-lived webhook echoes of our own text replies.
    45	        recentOutbound sync.Map // conversationID + "\x00" + normalized content → time.Time
    46	
    47	        stopCh  chan struct{}
    48	        stopCtx context.Context
    49	        stopFn  context.CancelFunc
    50	}
    51	
    52	// New creates a Pancake Channel from parsed credentials and config.
    53	func New(cfg pancakeInstanceConfig, creds pancakeCreds,
    54	        msgBus *bus.MessageBus, _ store.PairingStore) (*Channel, error) {
    55	
    56	        if creds.APIKey == "" {
    57	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: api_key is required")
    58	        }
    59	        if creds.PageAccessToken == "" {
    60	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: page_access_token is required")
    61	        }
    62	        if cfg.PageID == "" {
    63	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: page_id is required")
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        base := channels.NewBaseChannel(channels.TypePancake, msgBus, cfg.AllowFrom)
    67	        stopCtx, stopFn := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
    68	
    69	        ch := &Channel{
    70	                BaseChannel:   base,
    71	                config:        cfg,
    72	                apiClient:     NewAPIClient(creds.APIKey, creds.PageAccessToken, cfg.PageID),
    73	                pageID:        cfg.PageID,
    74	                platform:      cfg.Platform,
    75	                webhookSecret: creds.WebhookSecret,
    76	                stopCh:        make(chan struct{}),
    77	                stopCtx:       stopCtx,
    78	                stopFn:        stopFn,
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        return ch, nil
    82	}
    83	
    84	// Factory creates a Pancake Channel from DB instance data.
    85	// Implements channels.ChannelFactory.
    86	func Factory(name string, creds json.RawMessage, cfg json.RawMessage,
    87	        msgBus *bus.MessageBus, pairingSvc store.PairingStore) (channels.Channel, error) {
    88	
    89	        var c pancakeCreds
    90	        if err := json.Unmarshal(creds, &c); err != nil {
    91	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: decode credentials: %w", err)
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        var ic pancakeInstanceConfig
    95	        if len(cfg) > 0 {
    96	                if err := json.Unmarshal(cfg, &ic); err != nil {
    97	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: decode config: %w", err)
    98	                }
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        ch, err := New(ic, c, msgBus, pairingSvc)
   102	        if err != nil {
   103	                return nil, err
   104	        }
   105	        ch.SetName(name)
   106	        return ch, nil
   107	}
   108	
   109	// Start connects the channel: verifies token, resolves platform, registers webhook.
   110	func (ch *Channel) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
   111	        ch.MarkStarting("connecting to Pancake page")
   112	
   113	        if err := ch.apiClient.VerifyToken(ctx); err != nil {
   114	                ch.MarkFailed("token invalid", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindAuth, false)
   115	                return err
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        // Resolve platform and page name from page metadata (best-effort — don't fail on this).
   119	        if ch.platform == "" || ch.pageName == "" {
   120	                if page, err := ch.apiClient.GetPage(ctx); err != nil {
   121	                        slog.Warn("pancake: could not resolve platform from page metadata", "page_id", ch.pageID, "err", err)
   122	                } else {
   123	                        if page.Platform != "" {
   124	                                ch.platform = page.Platform
   125	                        }
   126	                        if page.Name != "" {
   127	                                ch.pageName = page.Name
   128	                        }
   129	                }
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        if ch.webhookSecret == "" {
   133	                slog.Warn("security.pancake_webhook_no_secret",
   134	                        "page_id", ch.pageID,
   135	                        "note", "webhook_secret not configured; incoming webhook requests will not be authenticated")
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        globalRouter.register(ch)
   139	        ch.MarkHealthy("connected to page " + ch.pageID)
   140	        ch.SetRunning(true)
   141	
   142	        // Background goroutine: evict stale dedup entries to prevent memory growth.
   143	        go ch.runDedupCleaner()
   144	
   145	        slog.Info("pancake channel started",
   146	                "page_id", ch.pageID,
   147	                "platform", ch.platform,
   148	                "name", ch.Name())
   149	        return nil
   150	}
   151	
   152	// Stop gracefully shuts down the channel.
   153	func (ch *Channel) Stop(_ context.Context) error {
   154	        globalRouter.unregister(ch.pageID)
   155	        ch.stopFn()
   156	        close(ch.stopCh)
   157	        ch.SetRunning(false)
   158	        ch.MarkStopped("stopped")
   159	        slog.Info("pancake channel stopped", "page_id", ch.pageID, "name", ch.Name())
   160	        return nil
   161	}
   162	
   163	// Send delivers an outbound message via Pancake API.
   164	func (ch *Channel) Send(ctx context.Context, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
   165	        slog.Debug("pancake: Send called",
   166	                "page_id", ch.pageID,
   167	                "chat_id", msg.ChatID,
   168	                "content_len", len(msg.Content),
   169	                "platform", ch.platform,
   170	                "channel_name", ch.Name())
   171	
   172	        conversationID := msg.ChatID
   173	        if conversationID == "" {
   174	                return fmt.Errorf("pancake: chat_id (conversation_id) is required for outbound message")
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
   178	
   179	        // Handle media attachments.
   180	        attachmentIDs, err := ch.handleMediaAttachments(ctx, msg)
   181	        if err != nil {
   182	                slog.Warn("pancake: media upload failed, sending text only",
   183	                        "page_id", ch.pageID, "err", err)
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        // Pancake's official contract makes `message` and `content_ids` mutually exclusive.
   187	        // Deliver uploaded media first, then follow with text chunks if needed.
   188	        if len(attachmentIDs) > 0 {
   189	                if err := ch.apiClient.SendAttachmentMessage(ctx, conversationID, attachmentIDs); err != nil {
   190	                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
   191	                        return err
   192	                }
   193	                if text == "" {
   194	                        return nil
   195	                }
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        // Text-only: split into platform-appropriate chunks.
   199	        // Store echo fingerprints BEFORE sending so that webhook echoes arriving
   200	        // while the HTTP round-trip is in flight are already recognized as self-sent.
   201	        parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
   202	        for _, part := range parts {
   203	                ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
   204	        }
   205	        for _, part := range parts {
   206	                if err := ch.apiClient.SendMessage(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
   207	                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
   208	                        // Remove pre-stored echo fingerprints for unsent parts so they
   209	                        // don't suppress genuine customer messages that happen to match.
   210	                        ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
   211	                        return err
   212	                }
   213	        }
   214	        return nil
   215	}
   216	
   217	// BlockReplyEnabled returns the per-channel block_reply override (nil = inherit gateway default).
   218	func (ch *Channel) BlockReplyEnabled() *bool { return ch.config.BlockReply }
   219	
   220	// WebhookHandler returns the shared webhook path and global router as handler.
   221	// Only the first pancake instance mounts the route; others return ("", nil).
   222	func (ch *Channel) WebhookHandler() (string, http.Handler) {
   223	        return globalRouter.webhookRoute()
   224	}
   225	
   226	// handleAPIError maps Pancake API errors to channel health states.
   227	func (ch *Channel) handleAPIError(err error) {
   228	        if err == nil {
   229	                return
   230	        }
   231	        switch {
   232	        case isAuthError(err):
   233	                ch.MarkFailed("token expired or invalid", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindAuth, false)
   234	        case isRateLimitError(err):
   235	                ch.MarkDegraded("rate limited", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindNetwork, true)
   236	        default:
   237	                ch.MarkDegraded("api error", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindUnknown, true)
   238	        }
   239	}
   240	
   241	// maxMessageLength returns the platform-specific character limit.
   242	func (ch *Channel) maxMessageLength() int {
   243	        switch ch.platform {
   244	        case "tiktok":
   245	                return 500
   246	        case "instagram":
   247	                return 1000
   248	        case "facebook", "zalo":
   249	                return 2000
   250	        case "whatsapp":
   251	                return 4096
   252	        case "line":
   253	                return 5000
   254	        default:
   255	                return 2000
   256	        }
   257	}

    34	// NewAPIClient creates a new Pancake APIClient for the given page.
    35	func NewAPIClient(apiKey, pageAccessToken, pageID string) *APIClient {
    36	        return &APIClient{
    37	                pageV1BaseURL:   "https://pages.fm/api/public_api/v1",
    38	                pageV2BaseURL:   publicAPIBase,
    39	                userBaseURL:     userAPIBase,
    40	                pageAccessToken: pageAccessToken,

    43	                httpClient:      &http.Client{Timeout: httpTimeout},
    44	        }
    45	}

    48	func (c *APIClient) VerifyToken(ctx context.Context) error {
    49	        url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations?limit=1", c.pageV2BaseURL, c.pageID)
    50	        if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil); err != nil {
    51	                return fmt.Errorf("pancake: token verification failed: %w", err)
    52	        }
    53	        slog.Info("pancake: page token verified", "page_id", c.pageID)
    54	        return nil
    55	}

    57	// GetPage fetches page metadata including platform (facebook/zalo/instagram/tiktok/whatsapp/line).
    58	func (c *APIClient) GetPage(ctx context.Context) (*PageInfo, error) {
    59	        url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages", c.userBaseURL)
    60	        req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
    61	        if err != nil {
    62	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: build get-pages request: %w", err)
    63	        }
    64	        req.Header.Set("Authorization", "Bearer "+c.apiKey)
    65	        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
    66	
    67	        res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
    68	        if err != nil {
    69	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: get pages request failed: %w", err)
    70	        }
    71	        defer res.Body.Close()
    72	
    73	        body, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
    74	        if err != nil {
    75	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: read get-pages response: %w", err)
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        var result struct {
    79	                Data []PageInfo `json:"data"`
    80	        }
    81	        if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &result); err != nil {
    82	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse get-pages response: %w", err)
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        for i := range result.Data {
    86	                if result.Data[i].ID == c.pageID {
    87	                        return &result.Data[i], nil
    88	                }
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // Page not found in list — return minimal info without platform
    92	        slog.Warn("pancake: page not found in pages list, platform unknown", "page_id", c.pageID)
    93	        return &PageInfo{ID: c.pageID}, nil
    94	}

    97	func (c *APIClient) SendMessage(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {

   122	// UploadMedia uploads a file via multipart/form-data and returns the attachment ID.
   123	func (c *APIClient) UploadMedia(ctx context.Context, filename string, data io.Reader, contentType string) (string, error) {
   124	        var buf bytes.Buffer
   125	        mw := multipart.NewWriter(&buf)
   126	
   127	        fw, err := mw.CreateFormFile("file", filepath.Base(filename))
   128	        if err != nil {
   129	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: create form file: %w", err)
   130	        }
   131	        if _, err := io.Copy(fw, data); err != nil {
   132	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: copy file data: %w", err)
   133	        }
   134	        mw.Close()
   135	
   136	        url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/upload_contents", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID)
   137	        req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, &buf)
   138	        if err != nil {
   139	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: build upload request: %w", err)
   140	        }
   141	        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", mw.FormDataContentType())
   142	
   143	        res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
   144	        if err != nil {
   145	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: upload request failed: %w", err)
   146	        }
   147	        defer res.Body.Close()
   148	
   149	        respBody, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
   150	        if err != nil {
   151	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: read upload response: %w", err)
   152	        }
   153	
   154	        var uploadResp UploadResponse
   155	        if err := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &uploadResp); err != nil {
   156	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse upload response: %w", err)
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if uploadResp.ID == "" {
   160	                return "", fmt.Errorf("pancake: upload response missing attachment ID")
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        return uploadResp.ID, nil
   164	}

   166	// doRequest executes an authenticated HTTP request using the page_access_token.
   167	// Always drains and closes the response body to enable connection reuse.
   168	func (c *APIClient) doRequest(ctx context.Context, method, url string, body io.Reader) error {
   169	        req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, method, url, body)
   170	        if err != nil {
   171	                return err
   172	        }
   173	        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
   174	
   175	        res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
   176	        if err != nil {
   177	                return err
   178	        }
   179	        defer res.Body.Close()
   180	
   181	        // Always read the full body to allow HTTP connection reuse.
   182	        respBody, _ := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
   183	
   184	        if res.StatusCode >= 400 {
   185	                var apiErr apiError
   186	                if jsonErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &apiErr); jsonErr == nil && apiErr.Message != "" {
   187	                        return &apiErr
   188	                }
   189	                return fmt.Errorf("pancake: HTTP %d", res.StatusCode)
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        // Some Pancake endpoints return HTTP 200 with a JSON body carrying success=false.
   193	        // Treat these as application-level send failures instead of silent success.
   194	        var appResp struct {
   195	                Success *bool  `json:"success,omitempty"`
   196	                Message string `json:"message,omitempty"`
   197	        }
   198	        if err := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &appResp); err == nil && appResp.Success != nil && !*appResp.Success {
   199	                if appResp.Message != "" {
   200	                        return fmt.Errorf("pancake: %s", appResp.Message)
   201	                }
   202	                return fmt.Errorf("pancake: request reported success=false")
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        return nil
   206	}
   207	
   208	func (c *APIClient) newPageRequest(ctx context.Context, method, rawURL string, body io.Reader) (*http.Request, error) {
   209	        req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, method, rawURL, body)
   210	        if err != nil {
   211	                return nil, err
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        query := req.URL.Query()
   215	        query.Set("page_access_token", c.pageAccessToken)
   216	        req.URL.RawQuery = query.Encode()
   217	
   218	        // Keep the header for compatibility; official docs require the query token.
   219	        req.Header.Set("Authorization", "Bearer "+c.pageAccessToken)
   220	        return req, nil
   221	}
   222	
   223	// isAuthError checks if an error is an authentication/authorization failure.
   224	// Uses errors.As to handle wrapped errors consistently with Facebook channel pattern.
   225	func isAuthError(err error) bool {
   226	        var ae *apiError
   227	        if !errors.As(err, &ae) {
   228	                return false
   229	        }
   230	        return ae.Code == 401 || ae.Code == 403 || ae.Code == 4001 || ae.Code == 4003
   231	}
   232	
   233	// isRateLimitError checks if an error is a rate limit response.
   234	func isRateLimitError(err error) bool {
   235	        var ae *apiError
   236	        if !errors.As(err, &ae) {
   237	                return false
   238	        }
   239	        return ae.Code == 429 || ae.Code == 4029
   240	}

     2	
     3	import (

    12	// handleMessagingEvent converts a Pancake "messaging" webhook event to bus.InboundMessage.
    13	func (ch *Channel) handleMessagingEvent(data MessagingData) {
    14	        slog.Debug("pancake: handleMessagingEvent called",
    15	                "page_id", ch.pageID,
    16	                "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID,
    17	                "conversation_id", data.ConversationID,
    18	                "type", data.Type,
    19	                "platform", data.Platform,
    20	                "msg_id", data.Message.ID,
    21	                "content_len", len(data.Message.Content))
    22	
    23	        // Dedup by message ID to handle Pancake's at-least-once delivery.
    24	        // Skip dedup when message ID is empty — prevents shared slot "msg:" from
    25	        // silently dropping all subsequent empty-ID messages across conversations.
    26	        var dedupKey string
    27	        if data.Message.ID != "" {
    28	                dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("msg:%s", data.Message.ID)
    29	                if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
    30	                        slog.Info("pancake: duplicate message skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    31	                        return
    32	                }
    33	        }
    34	
    35	        // Prevent reply loops: skip messages sent by the page itself.
    36	        if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
    37	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page message",
    38	                        "page_id", ch.pageID,
    39	                        "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
    40	                return
    41	        }
    42	        if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
    43	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff message",
    44	                        "page_id", ch.pageID,
    45	                        "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID,
    46	                        "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
    47	                return
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
    51	                slog.Warn("pancake: message missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    52	                return
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        // Check echo BEFORE buildMessageContent adds the [From: ...] prefix.
    56	        // rememberOutboundEcho stores the raw outbound text; the prefix would cause a
    57	        // key mismatch and silently break loop detection.
    58	        if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
    59	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound echo",
    60	                        "page_id", ch.pageID,
    61	                        "conversation_id", data.ConversationID,
    62	                        "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    63	                return
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        content := buildMessageContent(data)
    67	
    68	        metadata := map[string]string{
    69	                "pancake_mode":      strings.ToLower(data.Type), // "inbox" or "comment"
    70	                "conversation_type": data.Type,
    71	                "platform":          data.Platform,
    72	                "conversation_id":   data.ConversationID,
    73	                "message_id":        dedupKey,
    74	                "display_name":      channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
    75	                "page_name":         ch.pageName,
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        ch.HandleMessage(
    79	                data.Message.SenderID,
    80	                data.ConversationID, // ChatID = conversation_id for reply routing
    81	                content,
    82	                nil, // media handled inline via content URLs
    83	                metadata,
    84	                "direct", // Pancake inbox conversations are always treated as direct messages
    85	        )
    86	
    87	        slog.Debug("pancake: inbound message published to bus",
    88	                "page_id", ch.pageID,
    89	                "conv_id", data.ConversationID,
    90	                "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID,
    91	                "platform", data.Platform,
    92	                "type", data.Type,
    93	                "channel_name", ch.Name(),
    94	        )
    95	}
    96	
    97	// buildMessageContent combines text content and attachment URLs into a single string.
    98	// Format: [From: {SenderID} ({SenderName})] {content}
    99	func buildMessageContent(data MessagingData) string {
   100	        parts := []string{}
   101	
   102	        if data.Message.Content != "" {
   103	                parts = append(parts, stripHTML(data.Message.Content))
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        for _, att := range data.Message.Attachments {
   107	                if att.URL != "" {
   108	                        parts = append(parts, att.URL)
   109	                }
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        body := strings.Join(parts, "\n")
   113	
   114	        if data.Message.SenderID != "" {
   115	                prefix := fmt.Sprintf("[From: %s (%s)]", data.Message.SenderID, data.Message.SenderName)
   116	                if body != "" {
   117	                        return prefix + " " + body
   118	                }
   119	                return prefix
   120	        }
   121	        return body
   122	}
   123	
   124	// stripHTML removes HTML tags and unescapes HTML entities from s.
   125	func stripHTML(s string) string {
   126	        s = htmlTagRe.ReplaceAllString(s, "")
   127	        return html.UnescapeString(strings.TrimSpace(s))
   128	}
   129	
   130	func isAssignedStaff(assigneeIDs []string, senderID string) bool {
   131	        if senderID == "" {
   132	                return false
   133	        }
   134	        for _, assigneeID := range assigneeIDs {
   135	                if assigneeID == senderID {
   136	                        return true
   137	                }
   138	        }
   139	        return false
   140	}
   141

    20	// verifyHMAC verifies a Pancake HMAC-SHA256 signature.
    21	// Expected header format: "sha256=<hex-digest>"
    22	func verifyHMAC(body []byte, secret, signature string) bool {
    23	        const prefix = "sha256="
    24	        if len(signature) <= len(prefix) {
    25	                return false
    26	        }
    27	        got, err := hex.DecodeString(signature[len(prefix):])
    28	        if err != nil {
    29	                return false
    30	        }
    31	        mac := hmac.New(sha256.New, []byte(secret))
    32	        mac.Write(body)
    33	        expected := mac.Sum(nil)
    34	        return hmac.Equal(got, expected)
    35	}
    36

    39	// webhookRouter routes incoming Pancake webhook events to the correct channel instance by page_id.
    40	// A single HTTP handler is shared across all pancake channel instances.
    41	type webhookRouter struct {
    42	        mu           sync.RWMutex
    43	        instances    map[string]*Channel // pageID → channel
    44	        routeHandled bool                // true after first webhookRoute() call
    45	}

    50	
    51	func (r *webhookRouter) register(ch *Channel) {
    52	        r.mu.Lock()
    53	        defer r.mu.Unlock()
    54	        r.instances[ch.pageID] = ch
    55	}
    56	
    57	func (r *webhookRouter) unregister(pageID string) {
    58	        r.mu.Lock()
    59	        defer r.mu.Unlock()
    60	        delete(r.instances, pageID)
    61	}

    63	// webhookRoute returns the path+handler on first call; ("", nil) for subsequent calls.
    64	// The HTTP mux retains the route once registered — routeHandled prevents duplicate mounts.
    65	func (r *webhookRouter) webhookRoute() (string, http.Handler) {
    66	        r.mu.Lock()
    67	        defer r.mu.Unlock()
    68	        if !r.routeHandled {
    69	                r.routeHandled = true
    70	                return webhookPath, r
    71	        }
    72	        return "", nil
    73	}

    75	// ServeHTTP is the shared handler for all Pancake page webhooks.

    77	func (r *webhookRouter) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {

    80	                "remote_addr", req.RemoteAddr,

   113	                return
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        // Resolve page_id: try top-level first, then data-level, then extract from conversation ID.

   118	        if pageID == "" {
   119	                pageID = data.PageID
   120	        }

   125	                }

   152	        }

   172	                        registered = append(registered, pid)

     1	package pancake
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "html"
     5	        "regexp"
     6	        "strings"
     7	        "time"
     8	)
     9	
    10	var (
    11	        htmlBreakTagRe = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)<br\b[^>]*\/?>`)
    12	        htmlCloseTagRe = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)</(?:div|p|li|ul|ol|h[1-6])>`)
    13	        htmlTagRe      = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)<[^>]+>`)
    14	)
    15	
    16	// isDup checks and records a dedup key. Returns true if the key was already seen.
    17	func (ch *Channel) isDup(key string) bool {
    18	        _, loaded := ch.dedup.LoadOrStore(key, time.Now())
    19	        return loaded
    20	}
    21	
    22	// splitMessage splits text into chunks no longer than maxLen Unicode code points.
    23	// Operates on runes (not bytes) to avoid splitting multi-byte characters (CJK, emoji, Vietnamese).
    24	func splitMessage(text string, maxLen int) []string {
    25	        runes := []rune(text)
    26	        if maxLen <= 0 || len(runes) <= maxLen {
    27	                return []string{text}
    28	        }
    29	        var parts []string
    30	        for len(runes) > maxLen {
    31	                parts = append(parts, string(runes[:maxLen]))
    32	                runes = runes[maxLen:]
    33	        }
    34	        if len(runes) > 0 {
    35	                parts = append(parts, string(runes))
    36	        }
    37	        return parts
    38	}
    39	
    40	func (ch *Channel) forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, content string) {
    41	        if conversationID == "" {
    42	                return
    43	        }
    44	        normalized := normalizeEchoContent(content)
    45	        if normalized == "" {
    46	                return
    47	        }
    48	        ch.recentOutbound.Delete(conversationID + "\x00" + normalized)
    49	}
    50	
    51	func (ch *Channel) rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, content string) {
    52	        if conversationID == "" {
    53	                return
    54	        }
    55	        normalized := normalizeEchoContent(content)
    56	        if normalized == "" {
    57	                return
    58	        }
    59	        ch.recentOutbound.Store(conversationID+"\x00"+normalized, time.Now())
    60	}
    61	
    62	func (ch *Channel) isRecentOutboundEcho(conversationID, content string) bool {
    63	        if conversationID == "" {
    64	                return false
    65	        }
    66	        normalized := normalizeEchoContent(content)
    67	        if normalized == "" {
    68	                return false
    69	        }
    70	        key := conversationID + "\x00" + normalized
    71	        v, ok := ch.recentOutbound.Load(key)
    72	        if !ok {
    73	                return false
    74	        }
    75	        ts, ok := v.(time.Time)
    76	        if !ok {
    77	                ch.recentOutbound.Delete(key)
    78	                return false
    79	        }
    80	        if time.Since(ts) > outboundEchoTTL {
    81	                ch.recentOutbound.Delete(key)
    82	                return false
    83	        }
    84	        return true
    85	}
    86	
    87	func normalizeEchoContent(content string) string {
    88	        content = strings.TrimSpace(content)
    89	        if content == "" {
    90	                return ""
    91	        }
    92	
    93	        content = html.UnescapeString(content)
    94	        content = strings.ReplaceAll(content, "\r\n", "\n")
    95	        content = strings.ReplaceAll(content, "\r", "\n")
    96	        content = htmlBreakTagRe.ReplaceAllString(content, "\n")
    97	        content = htmlCloseTagRe.ReplaceAllString(content, "\n")
    98	        content = htmlTagRe.ReplaceAllString(content, "")
    99	
   100	        lines := strings.Split(content, "\n")
   101	        normalized := make([]string, 0, len(lines))
   102	        pendingBlank := false
   103	        for _, line := range lines {
   104	                line = strings.Join(strings.Fields(line), " ")
   105	                if line == "" {
   106	                        if len(normalized) == 0 || pendingBlank {
   107	                                continue
   108	                        }
   109	                        pendingBlank = true
   110	                        continue
   111	                }
   112	                if pendingBlank {
   113	                        normalized = append(normalized, "")
   114	                        pendingBlank = false
   115	                }
   116	                normalized = append(normalized, line)
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        return strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(normalized, "\n"))
   120	}
   121	
   122	// runDedupCleaner evicts dedup entries older than dedupTTL every dedupCleanEvery.
   123	func (ch *Channel) runDedupCleaner() {
   124	        ticker := time.NewTicker(dedupCleanEvery)
   125	        defer ticker.Stop()
   126	        for {
   127	                select {
   128	                case <-ch.stopCh:
   129	                        return
   130	                case <-ticker.C:
   131	                        now := time.Now()
   132	                        ch.dedup.Range(func(k, v any) bool {
   133	                                if t, ok := v.(time.Time); ok && now.Sub(t) > dedupTTL {
   134	                                        ch.dedup.Delete(k)
   135	                                }
   136	                                return true
   137	                        })
   138	                        ch.recentOutbound.Range(func(k, v any) bool {
   139	                                if t, ok := v.(time.Time); ok && now.Sub(t) > outboundEchoTTL {
   140	                                        ch.recentOutbound.Delete(k)
   141	                                }
   142	                                return true
   143	                        })
   144	                }
   145	        }
   146	}

   144	// CacheInvalidatePayload signals cache layers to evict stale entries.
   145	// Used with protocol.EventCacheInvalidate events. Events are delivered
   146	// in-process via MessageBus and never marshaled to the wire, so the json
   147	// tags are documentation-only (and omitempty on uuid.UUID is a no-op
   148	// because uuid.UUID is [16]byte — all-zero arrays don't count as empty).
   149	type CacheInvalidatePayload struct {

   151	        Key  string `json:"key"`  // agent_key, agent_id, etc. Empty = invalidate all

   153	        // global (master admin action) — subscribers treat it as "invalidate all".
   154	        TenantID uuid.UUID `json:"tenant_id"`

   175	        PublishOutbound(msg OutboundMessage)
   176	        SubscribeOutbound(ctx context.Context) (OutboundMessage, bool)

   179	// IsInternalSender returns true if the senderID belongs to an internal system
   180	// component (not a real channel user). These should not be stored as contacts.
   181	func IsInternalSender(senderID string) bool {
   182	        return strings.HasPrefix(senderID, "system:") ||
   183	                strings.HasPrefix(senderID, "notification:") ||
   184	                strings.HasPrefix(senderID, "teammate:") ||
   185	                strings.HasPrefix(senderID, "ticker:") ||
   186	                senderID == "session_send_tool"
   187	}

   148	// Stop gracefully shuts down the channel.
   149	func (ch *Channel) Stop(_ context.Context) error {
   150	        globalRouter.unregister(ch.pageID)
   151	        ch.stopFn()           // cancel stopCtx → cancels inflight Graph API calls
   152	        close(ch.stopCh)      // stop background goroutines
   153	        ch.SetRunning(false)
   154	        ch.MarkStopped("stopped")
   155	        slog.Info("facebook channel stopped", "page_id", ch.pageID, "name", ch.Name())
   156	        return nil
   157	}
   158	
   159	// Send delivers an outbound message. Dispatches to comment reply or Messenger based on fb_mode metadata.
   160	func (ch *Channel) Send(ctx context.Context, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
   161	        mode := msg.Metadata["fb_mode"]
   162	
   163	        switch mode {
   164	        case "messenger":
   165	                text := FormatForMessenger(msg.Content)
   166	                parts := splitMessage(text, messengerMaxChars)
   167	                for _, part := range parts {
   168	                        if _, err := ch.graphClient.SendMessage(ctx, msg.ChatID, part); err != nil {
   169	                                ch.handleAPIError(err)
   170	                                return err
   171	                        }
   172	                }
   173	
   174	        default: // "comment"
   175	                commentID := msg.Metadata["reply_to_comment_id"]
   176	                if commentID == "" {
   177	                        return fmt.Errorf("facebook: reply_to_comment_id missing in outbound metadata")
   178	                }
   179	                text := FormatForComment(msg.Content)
   180	                if _, err := ch.graphClient.ReplyToComment(ctx, commentID, text); err != nil {
   181	                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
   182	                        return err
   183	                }
   184	
   185	                // First inbox: send a private DM after comment reply (best-effort).
   186	                if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
   187	                        senderID := msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
   188	                        if senderID != "" {
   189	                                ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, senderID)
   190	                        }
   191	                }
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        return nil
   195	}
   196	
   197	// WebhookHandler returns the shared webhook path and the global router as handler.
   198	// Only the first facebook instance mounts the route; others return ("", nil).
   199	func (ch *Channel) WebhookHandler() (string, http.Handler) {
   200	        return globalRouter.webhookRoute()
   201	}
   202	
   203	// handleAPIError maps Graph API errors to channel health states.
   204	func (ch *Channel) handleAPIError(err error) {
   205	        if err == nil {
   206	                return
   207	        }
   208	        switch {
   209	        case IsAuthError(err):
   210	                ch.MarkFailed("token expired", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindAuth, false)
   211	        case IsPermissionError(err):
   212	                ch.MarkFailed("permission denied", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindAuth, false)
   213	        case IsRateLimitError(err):
   214	                ch.MarkDegraded("rate limited", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindNetwork, true)
   215	        default:
   216	                ch.MarkDegraded("api error", err.Error(), channels.ChannelFailureKindUnknown, true)
   217	        }
   218	}
   219	
   220	// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private DM after a comment reply (best-effort).

   220	// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private DM after a comment reply (best-effort).
   221	func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, senderID string) {
   222	        if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
   223	                return
   224	        }
   225	        message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
   226	        if message == "" {
   227	                message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
   228	        }
   229	        if _, err := ch.graphClient.SendMessage(ctx, senderID, message); err != nil {
   230	                slog.Warn("facebook: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "err", err)
   231	                ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
   232	        }
   233	}
   234	
   235	// runDedupCleaner evicts dedup entries older than dedupTTL every dedupCleanEvery.
   236	func (ch *Channel) runDedupCleaner() {
   237	        ticker := time.NewTicker(dedupCleanEvery)
   238	        defer ticker.Stop()
   239	        for {
   240	                select {
   241	                case <-ch.stopCh:
   242	                        return
   243	                case <-ticker.C:
   244	                        now := time.Now()
   245	                        ch.dedup.Range(func(k, v any) bool {
   246	                                if t, ok := v.(time.Time); ok && now.Sub(t) > dedupTTL {
   247	                                        ch.dedup.Delete(k)
   248	                                }
   249	                                return true
   250	                        })
   251	                }
   252	        }
   253	}
   254	
   255	// isDup checks and records a dedup key. Returns true if the key was already seen.
   256	func (ch *Channel) isDup(key string) bool {
   257	        _, loaded := ch.dedup.LoadOrStore(key, time.Now())
   258	        return loaded
   259	}

   110	type GraphComment struct {
   111	        ID          string `json:"id"`
   112	        Message     string `json:"message"`
   113	        From        FBUser `json:"from"`
   114	        CreatedTime string `json:"created_time"`
   115	}
   116	
   117	// GraphPost is a Facebook post object from the Graph API.
   118	type GraphPost struct {
   119	        ID          string `json:"id"`
   120	        Message     string `json:"message"`
   121	        Story       string `json:"story,omitempty"`
   122	        CreatedTime string `json:"created_time"`
   123	}
   124	
   125	// GraphPaging holds cursor-based pagination for Graph API list responses.
   126	type GraphPaging struct {
   127	        Cursors struct {
   128	                Before string `json:"before"`
   129	                After  string `json:"after"`
   130	        } `json:"cursors"`
   131	        Next string `json:"next,omitempty"`
   132	}
   133	
   134	// GraphListResponse is a generic Graph API list response.
   135	type GraphListResponse[T any] struct {
   136	        Data   []T         `json:"data"`
   137	        Paging GraphPaging `json:"paging,omitempty"`
   138	}
   139

   141	type graphErrorBody struct {
   142	        Error struct {

   144	                Type    string `json:"type"`

     1	package facebook
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "fmt"
     5	        "log/slog"
     6	        "strings"
     7	)
     8	
     9	// handleCommentEvent processes a feed webhook change where item == "comment".
    10	func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(entry WebhookEntry, change ChangeValue) {
    11	        // Feature gate.
    12	        if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
    13	                return
    14	        }
    15	
    16	        // Only process new comments (not edits or deletions).
    17	        if change.Verb != "add" {
    18	                return
    19	        }
    20	
    21	        // Page routing: ensure this event belongs to our page instance (before dedup write).
    22	        if entry.ID != ch.pageID {
    23	                return
    24	        }
    25	
    26	        // Self-reply prevention: skip comments posted by the page itself.
    27	        if change.From.ID == ch.pageID {
    28	                return
    29	        }
    30	
    31	        // Dedup: Facebook may deliver the same event more than once.
    32	        if ch.isDup("comment:" + change.CommentID) {
    33	                slog.Debug("facebook: duplicate comment event skipped", "comment_id", change.CommentID)
    34	                return
    35	        }
    36	
    37	        // Build message content — optionally enriched with post + thread context.
    38	        // Use stopCtx so inflight Graph API calls are cancelled when the channel stops.
    39	        content := change.Message
    40	        if ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.IncludePostContext && change.PostID != "" {
    41	                content = ch.buildEnrichedContent(change)
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        senderID := change.From.ID
    45	        // Session key groups all comments by the same user on the same post.
    46	        chatID := fmt.Sprintf("%s:%s", change.PostID, senderID)
    47	
    48	        metadata := map[string]string{
    49	                "comment_id":          change.CommentID,
    50	                "post_id":             change.PostID,
    51	                "parent_id":           change.ParentID,
    52	                "sender_name":         change.From.Name,
    53	                "sender_id":           senderID,
    54	                "fb_mode":             "comment",
    55	                "reply_to_comment_id": change.CommentID,
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        ch.HandleMessage(senderID, chatID, content, nil, metadata, "direct")
    59	}
    60	
    61	// buildEnrichedContent fetches post content and comment thread, assembles a rich
    62	// context string for the agent. Uses stopCtx so it is cancelled on channel Stop().
    63	func (ch *Channel) buildEnrichedContent(change ChangeValue) string {
    64	        ctx := ch.stopCtx
    65	
    66	        var sb strings.Builder
    67	
    68	        // Post content.
    69	        post, err := ch.postFetcher.GetPost(ctx, change.PostID)
    70	        if err == nil && post != nil && post.Message != "" {
    71	                sb.WriteString("[Bài đăng] ")
    72	                sb.WriteString(post.Message)
    73	                sb.WriteString("\n\n")
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        // Comment thread (when this is a nested reply).
    77	        if change.ParentID != "" {
    78	                depth := ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.MaxThreadDepth
    79	                if depth <= 0 {
    80	                        depth = 10
    81	                }
    82	                thread, err := ch.postFetcher.GetCommentThread(ctx, change.ParentID, depth)
    83	                if err == nil && len(thread) > 0 {
    84	                        sb.WriteString("[Thread]\n")
    85	                        for _, c := range thread {
    86	                                sb.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("- %s: %s\n", c.From.Name, c.Message))
    87	                        }
    88	                        sb.WriteString("\n")
    89	                }
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        // Current comment.
    93	        sb.WriteString("[Comment mới] ")
    94	        sb.WriteString(change.From.Name)
    95	        sb.WriteString(": ")
    96	        sb.WriteString(change.Message)
    97	
    98	        return sb.String()
    99	}

     1	package facebook
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"
     5	        "sync"
     6	        "time"
     7	
     8	        "golang.org/x/sync/singleflight"
     9	)
    10	
    11	const defaultPostCacheTTL = 15 * time.Minute
    12	
    13	// postCacheEntry holds a cached post with its expiry time.
    14	type postCacheEntry struct {
    15	        post      *GraphPost
    16	        expiresAt time.Time
    17	}
    18	
    19	// PostFetcher fetches and caches Facebook post content and comment threads.
    20	// singleflight prevents redundant concurrent Graph API calls for the same post
    21	// (cache stampede on viral posts receiving many comments simultaneously).
    22	type PostFetcher struct {
    23	        graphClient *GraphClient
    24	        cacheTTL    time.Duration
    25	        cache       sync.Map          // postID(string) → *postCacheEntry
    26	        sfGroup     singleflight.Group // coalesces concurrent fetches for the same postID
    27	}
    28	
    29	// NewPostFetcher creates a PostFetcher with the given cache TTL string (e.g. "15m").
    30	// Falls back to defaultPostCacheTTL if the string is empty or unparseable.
    31	func NewPostFetcher(client *GraphClient, cacheTTLStr string) *PostFetcher {
    32	        ttl := defaultPostCacheTTL
    33	        if cacheTTLStr != "" {
    34	                if d, err := time.ParseDuration(cacheTTLStr); err == nil && d > 0 {
    35	                        ttl = d
    36	                }
    37	        }
    38	        return &PostFetcher{
    39	                graphClient: client,
    40	                cacheTTL:    ttl,
    41	        }
    42	}
    43	
    44	// GetPost returns the post for postID, using cache when fresh.
    45	// Concurrent callers for the same postID share one inflight request.
    46	func (pf *PostFetcher) GetPost(ctx context.Context, postID string) (*GraphPost, error) {
    47	        if postID == "" {
    48	                return nil, nil
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        // Check cache first.
    52	        if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(postID); ok {
    53	                entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
    54	                if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
    55	                        return entry.post, nil
    56	                }
    57	                pf.cache.Delete(postID)
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        // Coalesce concurrent fetches for the same postID.
    61	        val, err, _ := pf.sfGroup.Do(postID, func() (any, error) {
    62	                // Re-check cache inside the singleflight call (another goroutine may have populated it).
    63	                if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(postID); ok {
    64	                        entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
    65	                        if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
    66	                                return entry.post, nil
    67	                        }
    68	                }
    69	                post, err := pf.graphClient.GetPost(ctx, postID)
    70	                if err != nil {
    71	                        return nil, err
    72	                }
    73	                pf.cache.Store(postID, &postCacheEntry{
    74	                        post:      post,
    75	                        expiresAt: time.Now().Add(pf.cacheTTL),
    76	                })
    77	                return post, nil
    78	        })
    79	        if err != nil {
    80	                return nil, err
    81	        }
    82	        if val == nil {
    83	                return nil, nil
    84	        }
    85	        return val.(*GraphPost), nil
    86	}
    87	
    88	// GetCommentThread fetches up to depth comments under parentCommentID.
    89	// Not cached — thread content changes frequently as replies arrive.
    90	func (pf *PostFetcher) GetCommentThread(ctx context.Context, parentCommentID string, depth int) ([]GraphComment, error) {
    91	        if parentCommentID == "" {
    92	                return nil, nil
    93	        }
    94	        return pf.graphClient.GetCommentThread(ctx, parentCommentID, depth)
    95	}
    96

   291	type captureTransport struct {
   292	        req  *http.Request
   293	        body []byte
   294	        resp *http.Response
   295	}
   296	
   297	func (t *captureTransport) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
   298	        t.req = req.Clone(req.Context())
   299	        if req.Body != nil {
   300	                body, err := io.ReadAll(req.Body)
   301	                if err != nil {
   302	                        return nil, err
   303	                }
   304	                t.body = body
   305	                req.Body = io.NopCloser(bytes.NewReader(body))
   306	        }
   307	        if t.resp != nil {
   308	                return t.resp, nil
   309	        }
   310	        return &http.Response{
   311	                StatusCode: http.StatusOK,
   312	                Header:     make(http.Header),
   313	                Body:       io.NopCloser(strings.NewReader(`{"success":true}`)),
   314	                Request:    req,
   315	        }, nil
   316	}

   375	// TestTruncateForTikTok_MultiByteCharacters verifies rune-safe truncation for
   376	// Vietnamese diacritics and emoji (multi-byte UTF-8 sequences).
   377	func TestTruncateForTikTok_MultiByteCharacters(t *testing.T) {
   378	        // Vietnamese text with diacritics (multi-byte UTF-8)
   379	        input := strings.Repeat("Xin chào ", 100) // ~900 bytes, <500 runes
   380	        result := truncateForTikTok(input)
   381	        if !utf8.ValidString(result) {
   382	                t.Fatal("truncateForTikTok produced invalid UTF-8")
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        // Emoji string exceeding 500 runes
   386	        emoji := strings.Repeat("😊", 600)
   387	        result = truncateForTikTok(emoji)
   388	        runes := []rune(result)
   389	        if len(runes) > 500 {
   390	                t.Errorf("expected <=500 runes, got %d", len(runes))
   391	        }
   392	        if !utf8.ValidString(result) {
   393	                t.Fatal("emoji truncation produced invalid UTF-8")
   394	        }
   395	}

   397	// TestMessageHandlerEmptyMessageID verifies that two messages with empty IDs
   398	// from different conversations are both published (not deduped against each other).
   399	func TestMessageHandlerEmptyMessageID(t *testing.T) {
   400	        msgBus := bus.New()
   401	        ch := &Channel{
   402	                BaseChannel: channels.NewBaseChannel(channels.TypePancake, msgBus, nil),
   403	                pageID:      "page-123",
   404	        }
   405	
   406	        // First message with empty ID — should be published
   407	        ch.handleMessagingEvent(MessagingData{
   408	                PageID: "page-123", ConversationID: "conv-1",
   409	                Type: "INBOX", Platform: "facebook",
   410	                Message: MessagingMessage{ID: "", SenderID: "user-1", Content: "hello"},
   411	        })
   412	
   413	        // Second message with empty ID, different conversation — should ALSO be published
   414	        ch.handleMessagingEvent(MessagingData{
   415	                PageID: "page-123", ConversationID: "conv-2",
   416	                Type: "INBOX", Platform: "facebook",
   417	                Message: MessagingMessage{ID: "", SenderID: "user-2", Content: "world"},
   418	        })
   419	
   420	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 100*time.Millisecond)
   421	        defer cancel()
   422	
   423	        _, ok1 := msgBus.ConsumeInbound(ctx)
   424	        if !ok1 {
   425	                t.Fatal("first empty-ID message should be published")
   426	        }
   427	        _, ok2 := msgBus.ConsumeInbound(ctx)
   428	        if !ok2 {
   429	                t.Fatal("second empty-ID message should NOT be deduped against first")
   430	        }
   431	}

362:func copyRoutingMeta(src map[string]string) map[string]string {
			// the answer stream (reasoning messages stay visible).
			rc.mu.Lock()
			currentStream := rc.stream
			rc.stream = nil
			rc.inToolPhase = true
			rc.thinkingDone = false    // allow new thinking in next iteration
			rc.thinkingBuffer = ""     // reset thinking buffer for new iteration
			rc.hasThinking = false     // new iteration starts fresh
			rc.tagParseSkipped = false // re-enable tag parsing for next iteration
			rc.mu.Unlock()
			if currentStream != nil {
				if err := currentStream.Stop(ctx); err != nil {
					slog.Debug("stream tool-phase stop failed", "channel", rc.ChannelName, "error", err)
				}
				// Don't finalize mid-run streams — their messageID must NOT go
				// into placeholders. Otherwise tool_status placeholder_update
				// overwrites streamed content, and subsequent FinalizeStream
				// calls overwrite the placeholder key, leaving earlier messages
				// stuck at tool status text. Only run.completed finalizes.
			}

			// Show tool status by editing placeholder message (non-streaming only).
			// Streaming channels show tool status via reaction emoji instead —
			// editing the placeholder would overwrite streamed content.
			toolName := extractPayloadString(payload, "name")
			if toolName != "" && rc.ToolStatusEnabled && !rc.Streaming {
				statusText := formatToolStatus(toolName)
				outMeta := copyRoutingMeta(rc.Metadata)
				outMeta["placeholder_update"] = "true"
				m.bus.PublishOutbound(bus.OutboundMessage{
					Channel:  rc.ChannelName,
					ChatID:   rc.ChatID,
					Content:  statusText,
					Metadata: outMeta,
				})
			}
		case protocol.ChatEventChunk:
			// Accumulate chunk deltas into full text.
			content := extractPayloadString(payload, "content")
			if content != "" {
				rc.mu.Lock()
				needNewStream := rc.inToolPhase
				if needNewStream {
					rc.streamBuffer = ""
					rc.inToolPhase = false
				}

				// Fallback <think> tag parsing: for providers that embed thinking
				// in the content stream (DeepSeek-via-OpenRouter, Qwen, some Ollama models).
				// Only activates when no native ChatEventThinking was received.
				if !rc.hasThinking && !rc.thinkingDone && !rc.tagParseSkipped {

     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "log/slog"
     7	        "strings"
     8	
     9	        "github.com/google/uuid"
    10

    13	        "github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/pkg/protocol"
    14	)
    15	
    16	// HandleAgentEvent routes agent lifecycle events to streaming/reaction channels.
    17	// Called from the bus event subscriber — must be non-blocking.
    18	// eventType: "run.started", "chunk", "tool.call", "tool.result", "run.completed", "run.failed", "run.cancelled"
    19	func (m *Manager) HandleAgentEvent(eventType, runID string, payload any) {
    20	        val, ok := m.runs.Load(runID)
    21	        if !ok {
    22	                return
    23	        }
    24	        rc := val.(*RunContext)
    25	
    26	        m.mu.RLock()
    27	        ch, exists := m.channels[rc.ChannelName]
    28	        m.mu.RUnlock()
    29	        if !exists {
    30	                return
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        ctx := context.Background()
    34	        if ta, ok := ch.(interface{ TenantID() uuid.UUID }); ok {
    35	                ctx = store.WithTenantID(ctx, ta.TenantID())
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        // Forward to StreamingChannel (only when streaming is enabled for this run).
    39	        // Without this gate, channels that implement StreamingChannel but have streaming
    40	        // disabled (e.g. group_stream=false) would create stream messages AND emit
    41	        // block.reply outbound messages, causing duplicate delivery.
    42	        if sc, ok := ch.(StreamingChannel); ok && rc.Streaming {
    43	                switch eventType {
    44	                case protocol.AgentEventRunStarted:
    45	                        stream, err := sc.CreateStream(ctx, rc.ChatID, true)
    46	                        if err != nil {
    47	                                slog.Debug("stream start failed", "channel", rc.ChannelName, "error", err)
    48	                        } else {
    49	                                rc.mu.Lock()
    50	                                rc.stream = stream
    51	                                rc.mu.Unlock()
    52	                        }
    53	                case protocol.ChatEventThinking:
    54	                        // Accumulate thinking/reasoning content and route to the current stream.
    55	                        // The stream created on run.started becomes the "reasoning lane":
    56	                        //  - DMs: edits the "Thinking..." placeholder with reasoning text
    57	                        //  - Groups: edits a fresh message with reasoning text
    58	                        // When the first chunk arrives, this stream is stopped (reasoning message stays
    59	                        // visible) and a new stream is created for the answer lane.
    60	                        // Gated by ReasoningStreamEnabled() — channels can opt out (e.g. Slack).
    61	                        if !sc.ReasoningStreamEnabled() {
    62	                                break
    63	                        }
    64	                        content := extractPayloadString(payload, "content")
    65	                        if content != "" {
    66	                                rc.mu.Lock()
    67	                                rc.thinkingBuffer += content
    68	                                rc.hasThinking = true
    69	                                thinkText := rc.thinkingBuffer
    70	                                currentStream := rc.stream
    71	                                rc.mu.Unlock()
    72	                                if currentStream != nil {
    73	                                        currentStream.Update(ctx, formatReasoningPreview(thinkText))
    74	                                }
    75	                        }
    76	                case protocol.AgentEventToolCall:
    77	                        // Agent is executing a tool — mark tool phase so the next chunk
    78	                        // (new LLM iteration) resets the stream buffer.
    79	                        // Stop the current stream (reasoning or answer) and finalize only
    80	                        // the answer stream (reasoning messages stay visible).

   572	// ValidatePolicy logs warnings for common policy misconfigurations.
   573	// Should be called during channel initialization.
   574	func (c *BaseChannel) ValidatePolicy(dmPolicy, groupPolicy string) {
   575	        if dmPolicy == "allowlist" && !c.HasAllowList() {
   576	                slog.Warn("channel policy misconfiguration: dmPolicy=allowlist but allowFrom is empty — all DMs will be rejected",
   577	                        "channel", c.name)
   578	        }
   579	        if groupPolicy == "allowlist" && !c.HasAllowList() {
   580	                slog.Warn("channel policy misconfiguration: groupPolicy=allowlist but allowFrom is empty — all group messages will be rejected",
   581	                        "channel", c.name)
   582	        }
   583	}
   584	
   585	// HandleMessage creates an InboundMessage and publishes it to the bus.
   586	// This is the standard way for channels to forward received messages.
   587	// peerKind should be "direct" or "group" (see sessions.PeerDirect, sessions.PeerGroup).
   588	func (c *BaseChannel) HandleMessage(senderID, chatID, content string, media []string, metadata map[string]string, peerKind string) {
   589	        // For DMs, enforce the allowlist as a safety net.
   590	        // For group messages, skip this check — group access is already enforced
   591	        // by the channel-specific group policy (checkGroupPolicy / CheckPolicy).
   592	        // Re-checking the sender here would incorrectly block users who are not
   593	        // individually listed but are in an allowed (or open-policy) group.
   594	        if peerKind != "group" && !c.IsAllowed(senderID) {
   595	                return
   596	        }
   597	
   598	        // Derive userID from senderID: strip "|username" suffix if present (legacy Slack compound format).
   599	        // All channels now pass plain senderID; kept for backward compat with stored compound IDs.
   600	        userID := senderID
   601	        if idx := strings.IndexByte(senderID, '|'); idx > 0 {
   602	                userID = senderID[:idx]
   603	        }
   604	
   605	        // Convert string paths to MediaFile (for channels that haven't been updated yet).
   606	        var mediaFiles []bus.MediaFile
   607	        for _, p := range media {
   608	                mediaFiles = append(mediaFiles, bus.MediaFile{Path: p})
   609	        }
   610	
   611	        msg := bus.InboundMessage{
   612	                Channel:  c.name,
   613	                SenderID: senderID,
   614	                ChatID:   chatID,
   615	                Content:  content,
   616	                Media:    mediaFiles,
   617	                PeerKind: peerKind,
   618	                UserID:   userID,
   619	                Metadata: metadata,
   620	                TenantID: c.tenantID,
   621	                AgentID:  c.agentID,
   622	        }
   623	
   624	        c.bus.PublishInbound(msg)
   625	}

     1	package channels
     2	
     3	// --- Run tracking for streaming/reaction event forwarding ---
     4	
     5	// RegisterRun associates a run ID with a channel context so agent events
     6	// (chunks, tool calls, completion) can be forwarded to the originating channel.
     7	func (m *Manager) RegisterRun(runID, channelName, chatID, messageID string, metadata map[string]string, streaming, blockReply, toolStatus bool) {
     8	        m.runs.Store(runID, &RunContext{
     9	                ChannelName:       channelName,
    10	                ChatID:            chatID,
    11	                MessageID:         messageID,
    12	                Metadata:          metadata,
    13	                Streaming:         streaming,
    14	                BlockReplyEnabled: blockReply,
    15	                ToolStatusEnabled: toolStatus,
    16	        })
    17	}
    18	
    19	// UnregisterRun removes a run tracking entry.
    20	func (m *Manager) UnregisterRun(runID string) {
    21	        m.runs.Delete(runID)
    22	}
    23	
    24	// IsStreamingChannel checks if a named channel implements StreamingChannel
    25	// AND has streaming currently enabled for the given chat type.
    26	// isGroup: true for group chats, false for DMs.
    27	func (m *Manager) IsStreamingChannel(channelName string, isGroup bool) bool {
    28	        m.mu.RLock()
    29	        ch, exists := m.channels[channelName]
    30	        m.mu.RUnlock()
    31	        if !exists {
    32	                return false
    33	        }
    34	        sc, ok := ch.(StreamingChannel)
    35	        if !ok {
    36	                return false
    37	        }
    38	        return sc.StreamEnabled(isGroup)
    39	}
    40	
    41	// ResolveBlockReply checks per-channel override, falls back to gateway default.
    42	// Returns true only if block.reply delivery should be enabled for this channel.
    43	func (m *Manager) ResolveBlockReply(channelName string, globalDefault *bool) bool {
    44	        m.mu.RLock()
    45	        ch, exists := m.channels[channelName]
    46	        m.mu.RUnlock()
    47	        if exists {
    48	                if bc, ok := ch.(BlockReplyChannel); ok {
    49	                        if v := bc.BlockReplyEnabled(); v != nil {
    50	                                return *v
    51	                        }
    52	                }
    53	        }
    54	        return globalDefault != nil && *globalDefault
    55	}

     1	package pancake
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "regexp"
     5	        "strings"
     6	)
     7	
     8	// FormatOutbound formats agent response text for the target platform.
     9	// Each platform has different formatting rules and supported markup.
    10	func FormatOutbound(content string, platform string) string {
    11	        switch platform {
    12	        case "facebook":
    13	                return formatForFacebook(content)
    14	        case "whatsapp":
    15	                return formatForWhatsApp(content)
    16	        case "zalo", "instagram", "line":
    17	                return stripMarkdown(content)
    18	        case "tiktok":
    19	                return stripMarkdown(truncateForTikTok(content))
    20	        default:
    21	                return stripMarkdown(content)
    22	        }
    23	}
    24	
    25	// formatForFacebook allows basic HTML tags supported by Messenger.
    26	// Strips unsupported tags, keeps bold/italic/links.
    27	func formatForFacebook(content string) string {
    28	        // Convert markdown bold (**text** or __text__) to plain (FB Messenger uses plain text)
    29	        content = reBold.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    30	        content = reItalic.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    31	        // Strip markdown code blocks and inline code
    32	        content = reCodeBlock.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    33	        content = reInlineCode.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    34	        // Strip markdown headers (## Heading → Heading)
    35	        content = reHeader.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    36	        return strings.TrimSpace(content)
    37	}
    38	
    39	// formatForWhatsApp converts markdown to WhatsApp-native formatting.
    40	// WhatsApp uses *bold*, _italic_, ~strikethrough~, ```code```.
    41	func formatForWhatsApp(content string) string {
    42	        // Convert **bold** → *bold* (WhatsApp format)
    43	        content = reDoubleBold.ReplaceAllString(content, "*$1*")
    44	        // Convert __italic__ → _italic_ (already matches WA format, just clean up __)
    45	        content = reDoubleUnderline.ReplaceAllString(content, "_$1_")
    46	        // Strip markdown headers
    47	        content = reHeader.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    48	        // Strip inline code backticks (keep content)
    49	        content = reInlineCode.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    50	        return strings.TrimSpace(content)
    51	}
    52	
    53	// stripMarkdown removes common markdown formatting, returning plain text.
    54	func stripMarkdown(content string) string {
    55	        content = reBold.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    56	        content = reItalic.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    57	        content = reCodeBlock.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    58	        content = reInlineCode.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    59	        content = reHeader.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    60	        content = reLink.ReplaceAllString(content, "$1")
    61	        content = reImage.ReplaceAllString(content, "")
    62	        return strings.TrimSpace(content)
    63	}
    64	
    65	// truncateForTikTok truncates content to TikTok DM limit (500 runes).
    66	// Uses rune slicing to avoid corrupting multi-byte UTF-8 (CJK, Vietnamese, emoji).
    67	func truncateForTikTok(content string) string {
    68	        const limit = 500
    69	        runes := []rune(content)
    70	        if len(runes) <= limit {
    71	                return content
    72	        }
    73	        return string(runes[:limit-3]) + "..."
    74	}
    75	
    76	// Compiled regexes for markdown stripping — package-level for efficiency.
    77	var (
    78	        reBold           = regexp.MustCompile(`(?:\*\*|__)(.+?)(?:\*\*|__)`)
    79	        reDoubleBold     = regexp.MustCompile(`\*\*(.+?)\*\*`)
    80	        reDoubleUnderline = regexp.MustCompile(`__(.+?)__`)
    81	        reItalic         = regexp.MustCompile(`(?:\*|_)(.+?)(?:\*|_)`)
    82	        reCodeBlock      = regexp.MustCompile("(?s)```(?:[a-z]*)?\n?(.+?)```")
    83	        reInlineCode     = regexp.MustCompile("`(.+?)`")
    84	        reHeader         = regexp.MustCompile(`(?m)^#{1,6}\s+(.+)$`)
    85	        reLink           = regexp.MustCompile(`\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)`)
    86	        reImage          = regexp.MustCompile(`!\[[^\]]*\]\([^)]+\)`)
    87	)
