func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
        text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
        if text == "" {
                return nil
        }

        parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
        for _, part := range parts {
                ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
        }
        for _, part := range parts {
                if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
                        ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
                        return err
                }
        }

        if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
                senderID := ""
                if msg.Metadata != nil {
                        senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
                }
                if senderID != "" {
                        ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
                }
        }
        return nil
}

// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
        if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
                return
        }
        message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
        if message == "" {
                message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
        }
        if err := ch.apiClient.PrivateReply(ctx, conversationID, message); err != nil {
                slog.Warn("pancake: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "conversation_id", conversationID, "err", err)
                ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
        }
}

func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
        text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
        if text == "" {
                return nil
        }

        parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
        for _, part := range parts {
                ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
        }
        for _, part := range parts {
                if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
                        ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
                        return err
                }
        }

// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
        if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
                return
        }
        message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage

        }

                ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
        }

func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
        text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
        if text == "" {
                return nil
        }

        parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
        for _, part := range parts {
                ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
        }
        for _, part := range parts {
                if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
                        ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
                        return err
                }
        }

        if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
                senderID := ""
                if msg.Metadata != nil {
                        senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
                }
                if senderID != "" {
                        ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
                }
        }
        return nil
}

// ListPosts lists recent posts for this page. Pancake'"'"'s public API exposes
// page posts as a collection; callers select the target post by ID.
func (c *APIClient) ListPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
        url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/posts", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID)
        req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: build list posts request: %w", err)
        }
        req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")

        res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: list posts request failed: %w", err)
        }
        defer res.Body.Close()

        respBody, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: read list posts response: %w", err)
        }
        if res.StatusCode >= 400 {
                var apiErr apiError
                if jsonErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &apiErr); jsonErr == nil && apiErr.Message != "" {
                        return nil, &apiErr
                }
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: HTTP %d", res.StatusCode)
        }

        var result struct {
                Data  []PostInfo `json:"data"`
                Posts []PostInfo `json:"posts"`
        }
        if err := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &result); err != nil {
                var direct []PostInfo
                if arrErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &direct); arrErr == nil {
                        return direct, nil
                }
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse list posts response: %w", err)
        }
        if len(result.Data) > 0 {
                return result.Data, nil
        }
        return result.Posts, nil
}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/internal/channels/pancake/post_fetcher.go --file_text 'package pancake

import (
        "context"
        "sync"
        "time"

        "golang.org/x/sync/singleflight"
)

const defaultPostCacheTTL = 15 * time.Minute

type postCacheEntry struct {
        posts     []PostInfo
        expiresAt time.Time
}

// PostFetcher fetches and caches Pancake page posts. Pancake exposes posts as a
// page-level collection, so singleflight uses a single "posts" key instead of a
// per-postID key to avoid stampedes when many comments arrive concurrently.
type PostFetcher struct {
        apiClient *APIClient
        cacheTTL  time.Duration
        cache     sync.Map
        sfGroup   singleflight.Group
}

// NewPostFetcher creates a PostFetcher with the given cache TTL string (e.g. "15m").
func NewPostFetcher(client *APIClient, cacheTTLStr string) *PostFetcher {
        ttl := defaultPostCacheTTL
        if cacheTTLStr != "" {
                if d, err := time.ParseDuration(cacheTTLStr); err == nil && d > 0 {
                        ttl = d
                }
        }
        return &PostFetcher{apiClient: client, cacheTTL: ttl}
}

// GetPost returns the post for postID, using a TTL cache of the page'"'"'s posts list.
func (pf *PostFetcher) GetPost(ctx context.Context, postID string) (*PostInfo, error) {
        if postID == "" || pf == nil || pf.apiClient == nil {
                return nil, nil
        }

        posts, err := pf.getPosts(ctx)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }
        for i := range posts {
                if posts[i].ID == postID {
                        return &posts[i], nil
                }
        }
        return nil, nil
}

func (pf *PostFetcher) getPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
        const key = "posts"
        if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
                entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
                if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
                        return entry.posts, nil
                }
                pf.cache.Delete(key)
        }

        val, err, _ := pf.sfGroup.Do(key, func() (any, error) {
                if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
                        entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
                        if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
                                return entry.posts, nil
                        }
                }
                posts, err := pf.apiClient.ListPosts(ctx)
                if err != nil {
                        return nil, err
                }
                pf.cache.Store(key, &postCacheEntry{
                        posts:     posts,
                        expiresAt: time.Now().Add(pf.cacheTTL),
                })
                return posts, nil
        })
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }
        if val == nil {
                return nil, nil
        }
        return val.([]PostInfo), nil
}

func postText(post *PostInfo) string {
        if post == nil {
                return ""
        }
        switch {
        case post.Message != "":
                return post.Message
        case post.Content != "":
                return post.Content
        case post.Caption != "":
                return post.Caption
        case post.Description != "":
                return post.Description
        default:
                return post.OriginalMessage
        }
}
'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/internal/channels/pancake/comment_handler.go --file_text 'package pancake

import (
        "fmt"
        "log/slog"
        "strings"

        "github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/channels"
)

// handleCommentEvent routes Pancake COMMENT conversations through the agent pipeline.
func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(data MessagingData) {
        if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
                return
        }

        // Dedup and echo/self checks must run before content enrichment so outbound
        // echo matching compares the raw webhook text rather than a prefixed body.
        var dedupKey string
        if data.Message.ID != "" {
                dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("comment:%s", data.Message.ID)
                if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
                        slog.Debug("pancake: duplicate comment skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
                        return
                }
        }

        if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
                slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
                return
        }
        if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
                slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
                return
        }
        if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
                slog.Warn("pancake: comment missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
                return
        }
        if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
                slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound comment echo", "page_id", ch.pageID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID, "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
                return
        }
        if !ch.commentPassesFilter(data.Message.Content) {
                return
        }

        content := ch.buildCommentContent(data)
        commentID := data.CommentID
        if commentID == "" {
                commentID = data.Message.ID
        }

        metadata := map[string]string{
                "pancake_mode":        "comment",
                "conversation_type":   data.Type,
                "platform":            data.Platform,
                "conversation_id":     data.ConversationID,
                "message_id":          dedupKey,
                "comment_id":          commentID,
                "post_id":             data.PostID,
                "parent_id":           data.ParentID,
                "sender_id":           data.Message.SenderID,
                "sender_name":         data.Message.SenderName,
                "display_name":        channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
                "page_name":           ch.pageName,
                "reply_to_comment_id": commentID,
        }

        ch.HandleMessage(
                data.Message.SenderID,
                data.ConversationID,
                content,
                nil,
                metadata,
                "direct",
        )
}

func (ch *Channel) commentPassesFilter(content string) bool {
        opts := ch.config.CommentReplyOptions
        if !strings.EqualFold(opts.Filter, "keyword") {
                return true
        }
        needle := strings.ToLower(content)
        for _, kw := range opts.Keywords {
                kw = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(kw))
                if kw != "" && strings.Contains(needle, kw) {
                        return true
                }
        }
        return false
}

func (ch *Channel) buildCommentContent(data MessagingData) string {
        body := buildMessageContent(data)
        if !ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.IncludePostContext || data.PostID == "" || ch.postFetcher == nil {
                return body
        }

        post, err := ch.postFetcher.GetPost(ch.stopCtx, data.PostID)
        if err != nil {
                slog.Debug("pancake: fetch post context failed", "post_id", data.PostID, "err", err)
                return body
        }
        text := strings.TrimSpace(postText(post))
        if text == "" {
                return body
        }
        return "[Bài đăng] " + stripHTML(text) + "\n\n[Comment mới] " + body
}
'

     2

    10	
    11	// handleCommentEvent routes Pancake COMMENT conversations through the agent pipeline.
    12	func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(data MessagingData) {
    13	        if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
    14	                return
    15	        }
    16	
    17	        // Dedup and echo/self checks must run before content enrichment so outbound
    18	        // echo matching compares the raw webhook text rather than a prefixed body.
    19	        var dedupKey string
    20	        if data.Message.ID != "" {
    21	                dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("comment:%s", data.Message.ID)
    22	                if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
    23	                        slog.Debug("pancake: duplicate comment skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    24	                        return
    25	                }
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
    29	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
    30	                return
    31	        }
    32	        if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
    33	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
    34	                return
    35	        }
    36	        if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
    37	                slog.Warn("pancake: comment missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    38	                return
    39	        }
    40	        if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
    41	                slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound comment echo", "page_id", ch.pageID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID, "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
    42	                return
    43	        }
    44	        if !ch.commentPassesFilter(data.Message.Content) {
    45	                return
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        content := ch.buildCommentContent(data)
    49	        commentID := data.CommentID
    50	        if commentID == "" {
    51	                commentID = data.Message.ID
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        metadata := map[string]string{
    55	                "pancake_mode":        "comment",
    56	                "conversation_type":   data.Type,
    57	                "platform":            data.Platform,
    58	                "conversation_id":     data.ConversationID,
    59	                "message_id":          dedupKey,
    60	                "comment_id":          commentID,
    61	                "post_id":             data.PostID,
    62	                "parent_id":           data.ParentID,
    63	                "sender_id":           data.Message.SenderID,
    64	                "sender_name":         data.Message.SenderName,
    65	                "display_name":        channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
    66	                "page_name":           ch.pageName,
    67	                "reply_to_comment_id": commentID,
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        ch.HandleMessage(
    71	                data.Message.SenderID,
    72	                data.ConversationID,
    73	                content,
    74	                nil,
    75	                metadata,
    76	                "direct",
    77	        )
    78	}

   233	func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
   234	        text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
   235	        if text == "" {
   236	                return nil
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
   240	        for _, part := range parts {
   241	                ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
   242	        }
   243	        for _, part := range parts {
   244	                if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
   245	                        ch.handleAPIError(err)
   246	                        ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
   247	                        return err
   248	                }
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
   252	                senderID := ""
   253	                if msg.Metadata != nil {
   254	                        senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
   255	                }
   256	                if senderID != "" {
   257	                        ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
   258	                }
   259	        }
   260	        return nil
   261	}
   262	
   263	// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
   264	func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
   265	        if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
   266	                return
   267	        }
   268	        message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
   269	        if message == "" {
   270	                message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
   271	        }
   272	        if err := ch.apiClient.PrivateReply(ctx, conversationID, message); err != nil {
   273	                slog.Warn("pancake: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "conversation_id", conversationID, "err", err)
   274	                ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
   275	        }
   276	}

	for i, part := range parts {
		if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
			ch.handleAPIError(err)
			for _, unsent := range parts[i:] {
				ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, unsent)
			}
			return err
		}
	}'

func parsePostsResponse(body []byte) ([]PostInfo, error) {
        var direct []PostInfo
        if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &direct); err == nil {
                return direct, nil
        }

        var result struct {
                Data  json.RawMessage `json:"data"`
                Posts json.RawMessage `json:"posts"`
        }
        if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &result); err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }
        for _, raw := range []json.RawMessage{result.Data, result.Posts} {
                if len(raw) == 0 || string(raw) == "null" {
                        continue
                }
                if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &direct); err == nil {
                        return direct, nil
                }
                var nested struct {
                        Data  []PostInfo `json:"data"`
                        Posts []PostInfo `json:"posts"`
                }
                if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &nested); err == nil {
                        if len(nested.Data) > 0 {
                                return nested.Data, nil
                        }
                        if nested.Posts != nil {
                                return nested.Posts, nil
                        }
                }
        }
        return nil, nil
}

+// ReplyComment replies publicly to a social comment conversation.
+func (c *APIClient) ReplyComment(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "reply_comment",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: reply comment: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// PrivateReply sends a first-inbox private reply to a commenter.
+func (c *APIClient) PrivateReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "private_reply",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: private reply: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// ListPosts lists recent posts for this page. Pancake's public API exposes
+// page posts as a collection; callers select the target post by ID.
+func (c *APIClient) ListPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/posts", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID)
+	req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: build list posts request: %w", err)
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
+
+	res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: list posts request failed: %w", err)
+	}
+	defer res.Body.Close()
+
+	respBody, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: read list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	if res.StatusCode >= 400 {
+		var apiErr apiError
+		if jsonErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &apiErr); jsonErr == nil && apiErr.Message != "" {
+			return nil, &apiErr
+		}
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: HTTP %d", res.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	posts, err := parsePostsResponse(respBody)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	return posts, nil
+}
+
+func parsePostsResponse(body []byte) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	var direct []PostInfo
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &direct); err == nil {
+		return direct, nil
+	}
+
+	var result struct {
+		Data  json.RawMessage `json:"data"`
+		Posts json.RawMessage `json:"posts"`
+	}
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &result); err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for _, raw := range []json.RawMessage{result.Data, result.Posts} {
+		if len(raw) == 0 || string(raw) == "null" {
+			continue
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &direct); err == nil {
+			return direct, nil
+		}
+		var nested struct {
+			Data  []PostInfo `json:"data"`
+			Posts []PostInfo `json:"posts"`
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &nested); err == nil {
+			if len(nested.Data) > 0 {
+				return nested.Data, nil
+			}
+			if nested.Posts != nil {
+				return nested.Posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}

+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"fmt"
+	"log/slog"
+	"strings"
+
+	"github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/channels"
+)
+
+// handleCommentEvent routes Pancake COMMENT conversations through the agent pipeline.
+func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(data MessagingData) {
+	if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
+		return
+	}
+
+	// Dedup and echo/self checks must run before content enrichment so outbound
+	// echo matching compares the raw webhook text rather than a prefixed body.
+	var dedupKey string
+	if data.Message.ID != "" {
+		dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("comment:%s", data.Message.ID)
+		if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
+			slog.Debug("pancake: duplicate comment skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
+		return
+	}
+	if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
+		return
+	}
+	if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: comment missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound comment echo", "page_id", ch.pageID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID, "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if !ch.commentPassesFilter(data.Message.Content) {
+		return
+	}
+
+	content := ch.buildCommentContent(data)
+	commentID := data.CommentID
+	if commentID == "" {
+		commentID = data.Message.ID
+	}
+
+	metadata := map[string]string{
+		"pancake_mode":        "comment",
+		"conversation_type":   data.Type,
+		"platform":            data.Platform,
+		"conversation_id":     data.ConversationID,
+		"message_id":          dedupKey,
+		"comment_id":          commentID,
+		"post_id":             data.PostID,
+		"parent_id":           data.ParentID,
+		"sender_id":           data.Message.SenderID,
+		"sender_name":         data.Message.SenderName,
+		"display_name":        channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
+		"page_name":           ch.pageName,
+		"reply_to_comment_id": commentID,
+	}
+
+	ch.HandleMessage(
+		data.Message.SenderID,
+		data.ConversationID,
+		content,
+		nil,
+		metadata,
+		"direct",
+	)
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) commentPassesFilter(content string) bool {
+	opts := ch.config.CommentReplyOptions
+	if !strings.EqualFold(opts.Filter, "keyword") {
+		return true
+	}
+	needle := strings.ToLower(content)
+	for _, kw := range opts.Keywords {
+		kw = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(kw))
+		if kw != "" && strings.Contains(needle, kw) {
+			return true
+		}
+	}
+	return false
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) buildCommentContent(data MessagingData) string {
+	body := buildMessageContent(data)
+	if !ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.IncludePostContext || data.PostID == "" || ch.postFetcher == nil {
+		return body
+	}
+
+	post, err := ch.postFetcher.GetPost(ch.stopCtx, data.PostID)
+	if err != nil {
+		slog.Debug("pancake: fetch post context failed", "post_id", data.PostID, "err", err)
+		return body
+	}
+	text := strings.TrimSpace(postText(post))
+	if text == "" {
+		return body
+	}
+	return "[Bài đăng] " + stripHTML(text) + "\n\n[Comment mới] " + body
+}

+func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
+	text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
+	if text == "" {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
+	for _, part := range parts {
+		ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
+	}
+	for i, part := range parts {
+		if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
+			ch.handleAPIError(err)
+			for _, unsent := range parts[i:] {
+				ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, unsent)
+			}
+			return err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
+		senderID := ""
+		if msg.Metadata != nil {
+			senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
+		}
+		if senderID != "" {
+			ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
+func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
+	if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
+		return
+	}
+	message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
+	if message == "" {
+		message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
+	}
+	if err := ch.apiClient.PrivateReply(ctx, conversationID, message); err != nil {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "conversation_id", conversationID, "err", err)
+		ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
+	}
+}

+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"sync"
+	"time"
+
+	"golang.org/x/sync/singleflight"
+)
+
+const defaultPostCacheTTL = 15 * time.Minute
+
+type postCacheEntry struct {
+	posts     []PostInfo
+	expiresAt time.Time
+}
+
+// PostFetcher fetches and caches Pancake page posts. Pancake exposes posts as a
+// page-level collection, so singleflight uses a single "posts" key instead of a
+// per-postID key to avoid stampedes when many comments arrive concurrently.
+type PostFetcher struct {
+	apiClient *APIClient
+	cacheTTL  time.Duration
+	cache     sync.Map
+	sfGroup   singleflight.Group
+}
+
+// NewPostFetcher creates a PostFetcher with the given cache TTL string (e.g. "15m").
+func NewPostFetcher(client *APIClient, cacheTTLStr string) *PostFetcher {
+	ttl := defaultPostCacheTTL
+	if cacheTTLStr != "" {
+		if d, err := time.ParseDuration(cacheTTLStr); err == nil && d > 0 {
+			ttl = d
+		}
+	}
+	return &PostFetcher{apiClient: client, cacheTTL: ttl}
+}
+
+// GetPost returns the post for postID, using a TTL cache of the page's posts list.
+func (pf *PostFetcher) GetPost(ctx context.Context, postID string) (*PostInfo, error) {
+	if postID == "" || pf == nil || pf.apiClient == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+
+	posts, err := pf.getPosts(ctx)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for i := range posts {
+		if posts[i].ID == postID {
+			return &posts[i], nil
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+func (pf *PostFetcher) getPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	const key = "posts"
+	if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+		entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+		if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+			return entry.posts, nil
+		}
+		pf.cache.Delete(key)
+	}
+
+	val, err, _ := pf.sfGroup.Do(key, func() (any, error) {
+		if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+			entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+			if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+				return entry.posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+		posts, err := pf.apiClient.ListPosts(ctx)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+		pf.cache.Store(key, &postCacheEntry{
+			posts:     posts,
+			expiresAt: time.Now().Add(pf.cacheTTL),
+		})
+		return posts, nil
+	})
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	if val == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+	return val.([]PostInfo), nil
+}
+
+func postText(post *PostInfo) string {
+	if post == nil {
+		return ""
+	}
+	switch {
+	case post.Message != "":
+		return post.Message
+	case post.Content != "":
+		return post.Content
+	case post.Caption != "":
+		return post.Caption
+	case post.Description != "":
+		return post.Description
+	default:
+		return post.OriginalMessage
+	}
+}

+func firstNonEmpty(values ...string) string {
+	for _, v := range values {
+		if v != "" {
+			return v
+		}
+	}
+	return ""

+// ReplyComment replies publicly to a social comment conversation.
+func (c *APIClient) ReplyComment(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "reply_comment",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: reply comment: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// PrivateReply sends a first-inbox private reply to a commenter.
+func (c *APIClient) PrivateReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "private_reply",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: private reply: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// ListPosts lists recent posts for this page. Pancake's public API exposes
+// page posts as a collection; callers select the target post by ID.
+func (c *APIClient) ListPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/posts", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID)
+	req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: build list posts request: %w", err)
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
+
+	res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: list posts request failed: %w", err)
+	}
+	defer res.Body.Close()
+
+	respBody, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: read list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	if res.StatusCode >= 400 {
+		var apiErr apiError
+		if jsonErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &apiErr); jsonErr == nil && apiErr.Message != "" {
+			return nil, &apiErr
+		}
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: HTTP %d", res.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	posts, err := parsePostsResponse(respBody)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	return posts, nil
+}
+
+func parsePostsResponse(body []byte) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	var direct []PostInfo
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &direct); err == nil {
+		return direct, nil
+	}
+
+	var result struct {
+		Data  json.RawMessage `json:"data"`
+		Posts json.RawMessage `json:"posts"`
+	}
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &result); err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for _, raw := range []json.RawMessage{result.Data, result.Posts} {
+		if len(raw) == 0 || string(raw) == "null" {
+			continue
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &direct); err == nil {
+			return direct, nil
+		}
+		var nested struct {
+			Data  []PostInfo `json:"data"`
+			Posts []PostInfo `json:"posts"`
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &nested); err == nil {
+			if len(nested.Data) > 0 {
+				return nested.Data, nil
+			}
+			if nested.Posts != nil {
+				return nested.Posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}

 	var buf bytes.Buffer

+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"fmt"
+	"log/slog"
+	"strings"
+
+	"github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/channels"
+)
+
+// handleCommentEvent routes Pancake COMMENT conversations through the agent pipeline.
+func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(data MessagingData) {
+	if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
+		return
+	}
+
+	// Dedup and echo/self checks must run before content enrichment so outbound
+	// echo matching compares the raw webhook text rather than a prefixed body.
+	var dedupKey string
+	if data.Message.ID != "" {
+		dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("comment:%s", data.Message.ID)
+		if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
+			slog.Debug("pancake: duplicate comment skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
+		return
+	}
+	if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
+		return
+	}
+	if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: comment missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound comment echo", "page_id", ch.pageID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID, "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if !ch.commentPassesFilter(data.Message.Content) {
+		return
+	}
+
+	content := ch.buildCommentContent(data)
+	commentID := data.CommentID
+	if commentID == "" {
+		commentID = data.Message.ID
+	}
+
+	metadata := map[string]string{
+		"pancake_mode":        "comment",
+		"conversation_type":   data.Type,
+		"platform":            data.Platform,
+		"conversation_id":     data.ConversationID,
+		"message_id":          dedupKey,
+		"comment_id":          commentID,
+		"post_id":             data.PostID,
+		"parent_id":           data.ParentID,
+		"sender_id":           data.Message.SenderID,
+		"sender_name":         data.Message.SenderName,
+		"display_name":        channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
+		"page_name":           ch.pageName,
+		"reply_to_comment_id": commentID,
+	}
+
+	ch.HandleMessage(
+		data.Message.SenderID,
+		data.ConversationID,
+		content,
+		nil,
+		metadata,
+		"direct",
+	)
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) commentPassesFilter(content string) bool {
+	opts := ch.config.CommentReplyOptions
+	if !strings.EqualFold(opts.Filter, "keyword") {
+		return true
+	}
+	needle := strings.ToLower(content)
+	for _, kw := range opts.Keywords {
+		kw = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(kw))
+		if kw != "" && strings.Contains(needle, kw) {
+			return true
+		}
+	}
+	return false
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) buildCommentContent(data MessagingData) string {
+	body := buildMessageContent(data)
+	if !ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.IncludePostContext || data.PostID == "" || ch.postFetcher == nil {
+		return body
+	}
+
+	post, err := ch.postFetcher.GetPost(ch.stopCtx, data.PostID)
+	if err != nil {
+		slog.Debug("pancake: fetch post context failed", "post_id", data.PostID, "err", err)
+		return body
+	}
+	text := strings.TrimSpace(postText(post))
+	if text == "" {
+		return body
+	}
+	return "[Bài đăng] " + stripHTML(text) + "\n\n[Comment mới] " + body
+}

+func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
+	text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
+	if text == "" {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
+	for _, part := range parts {
+		ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
+	}
+	for i, part := range parts {
+		if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
+			ch.handleAPIError(err)
+			for _, unsent := range parts[i:] {
+				ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, unsent)
+			}
+			return err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
+		senderID := ""
+		if msg.Metadata != nil {
+			senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
+		}
+		if senderID != "" {
+			ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
+func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
+	if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
+		return
+	}
+	message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
+	if message == "" {
+		message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
+	}
+	if err := ch.apiClient.PrivateReply(ctx, conversationID, message); err != nil {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "conversation_id", conversationID, "err", err)
+		ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
+	}
+}

new file mode 100644
index 0000000..af1045f
--- /dev/null
+++ b/internal/channels/pancake/post_fetcher.go
@@ -0,0 +1,109 @@
+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"sync"
+	"time"
+
+	"golang.org/x/sync/singleflight"
+)
+
+const defaultPostCacheTTL = 15 * time.Minute
+
+type postCacheEntry struct {
+	posts     []PostInfo
+	expiresAt time.Time
+}
+
+// PostFetcher fetches and caches Pancake page posts. Pancake exposes posts as a
+// page-level collection, so singleflight uses a single "posts" key instead of a
+// per-postID key to avoid stampedes when many comments arrive concurrently.
+type PostFetcher struct {
+	apiClient *APIClient
+	cacheTTL  time.Duration
+	cache     sync.Map
+	sfGroup   singleflight.Group
+}
+
+// NewPostFetcher creates a PostFetcher with the given cache TTL string (e.g. "15m").
+func NewPostFetcher(client *APIClient, cacheTTLStr string) *PostFetcher {
+	ttl := defaultPostCacheTTL
+	if cacheTTLStr != "" {
+		if d, err := time.ParseDuration(cacheTTLStr); err == nil && d > 0 {
+			ttl = d
+		}
+	}
+	return &PostFetcher{apiClient: client, cacheTTL: ttl}
+}
+
+// GetPost returns the post for postID, using a TTL cache of the page's posts list.
+func (pf *PostFetcher) GetPost(ctx context.Context, postID string) (*PostInfo, error) {
+	if postID == "" || pf == nil || pf.apiClient == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+
+	posts, err := pf.getPosts(ctx)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for i := range posts {
+		if posts[i].ID == postID {
+			return &posts[i], nil
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+func (pf *PostFetcher) getPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	const key = "posts"
+	if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+		entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+		if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+			return entry.posts, nil
+		}
+		pf.cache.Delete(key)
+	}
+
+	val, err, _ := pf.sfGroup.Do(key, func() (any, error) {
+		if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+			entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+			if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+				return entry.posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+		posts, err := pf.apiClient.ListPosts(ctx)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+		pf.cache.Store(key, &postCacheEntry{
+			posts:     posts,
+			expiresAt: time.Now().Add(pf.cacheTTL),
+		})
+		return posts, nil
+	})
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	if val == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+	return val.([]PostInfo), nil
+}
+
+func postText(post *PostInfo) string {
+	if post == nil {
+		return ""
+	}
+	switch {
+	case post.Message != "":
+		return post.Message
+	case post.Content != "":
+		return post.Content
+	case post.Caption != "":
+		return post.Caption
+	case post.Description != "":
+		return post.Description
+	default:
+		return post.OriginalMessage
+	}
+}

+// ReplyComment replies publicly to a social comment conversation.
+func (c *APIClient) ReplyComment(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "reply_comment",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: reply comment: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// PrivateReply sends a first-inbox private reply to a commenter.
+func (c *APIClient) PrivateReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID, content string) error {
+	body, _ := json.Marshal(SendMessageRequest{
+		Action:  "private_reply",
+		Message: content,
+	})
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/conversations/%s/messages", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID, conversationID)
+	if err := c.doRequest(ctx, http.MethodPost, url, bytes.NewReader(body)); err != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("pancake: private reply: %w", err)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// ListPosts lists recent posts for this page. Pancake's public API exposes
+// page posts as a collection; callers select the target post by ID.
+func (c *APIClient) ListPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	url := fmt.Sprintf("%s/pages/%s/posts", c.pageV1BaseURL, c.pageID)
+	req, err := c.newPageRequest(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: build list posts request: %w", err)
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
+
+	res, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: list posts request failed: %w", err)
+	}
+	defer res.Body.Close()
+
+	respBody, err := io.ReadAll(res.Body)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: read list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	if res.StatusCode >= 400 {
+		var apiErr apiError
+		if jsonErr := json.Unmarshal(respBody, &apiErr); jsonErr == nil && apiErr.Message != "" {
+			return nil, &apiErr
+		}
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: HTTP %d", res.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	posts, err := parsePostsResponse(respBody)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("pancake: parse list posts response: %w", err)
+	}
+	return posts, nil
+}
+
+func parsePostsResponse(body []byte) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	var direct []PostInfo
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &direct); err == nil {
+		return direct, nil
+	}
+
+	var result struct {
+		Data  json.RawMessage `json:"data"`
+		Posts json.RawMessage `json:"posts"`
+	}
+	if err := json.Unmarshal(body, &result); err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for _, raw := range []json.RawMessage{result.Data, result.Posts} {
+		if len(raw) == 0 || string(raw) == "null" {
+			continue
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &direct); err == nil {
+			return direct, nil
+		}
+		var nested struct {
+			Data  []PostInfo `json:"data"`
+			Posts []PostInfo `json:"posts"`
+		}
+		if err := json.Unmarshal(raw, &nested); err == nil {
+			if len(nested.Data) > 0 {
+				return nested.Data, nil
+			}
+			if nested.Posts != nil {
+				return nested.Posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+

 	var buf bytes.Buffer

+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"fmt"
+	"log/slog"
+	"strings"
+
+	"github.com/nextlevelbuilder/goclaw/internal/channels"
+)
+
+// handleCommentEvent routes Pancake COMMENT conversations through the agent pipeline.
+func (ch *Channel) handleCommentEvent(data MessagingData) {
+	if !ch.config.Features.CommentReply {
+		return
+	}
+
+	// Dedup and echo/self checks must run before content enrichment so outbound
+	// echo matching compares the raw webhook text rather than a prefixed body.
+	var dedupKey string
+	if data.Message.ID != "" {
+		dedupKey = fmt.Sprintf("comment:%s", data.Message.ID)
+		if ch.isDup(dedupKey) {
+			slog.Debug("pancake: duplicate comment skipped", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	if data.Message.SenderID == ch.pageID {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping own page comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID)
+		return
+	}
+	if isAssignedStaff(data.AssigneeIDs, data.Message.SenderID) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping assigned staff comment", "page_id", ch.pageID, "sender_id", data.Message.SenderID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID)
+		return
+	}
+	if data.Message.SenderID == "" {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: comment missing sender_id, skipping", "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if ch.isRecentOutboundEcho(data.ConversationID, data.Message.Content) {
+		slog.Info("pancake: skipping recent outbound comment echo", "page_id", ch.pageID, "conversation_id", data.ConversationID, "msg_id", data.Message.ID)
+		return
+	}
+	if !ch.commentPassesFilter(data.Message.Content) {
+		return
+	}
+
+	content := ch.buildCommentContent(data)
+	commentID := data.CommentID
+	if commentID == "" {
+		commentID = data.Message.ID
+	}
+
+	metadata := map[string]string{
+		"pancake_mode":        "comment",
+		"conversation_type":   data.Type,
+		"platform":            data.Platform,
+		"conversation_id":     data.ConversationID,
+		"message_id":          dedupKey,
+		"comment_id":          commentID,
+		"post_id":             data.PostID,
+		"parent_id":           data.ParentID,
+		"sender_id":           data.Message.SenderID,
+		"sender_name":         data.Message.SenderName,
+		"display_name":        channels.SanitizeDisplayName(data.Message.SenderName),
+		"page_name":           ch.pageName,
+		"reply_to_comment_id": commentID,
+	}
+
+	ch.HandleMessage(
+		data.Message.SenderID,
+		data.ConversationID,
+		content,
+		nil,
+		metadata,
+		"direct",
+	)
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) commentPassesFilter(content string) bool {
+	opts := ch.config.CommentReplyOptions
+	if !strings.EqualFold(opts.Filter, "keyword") {
+		return true
+	}
+	needle := strings.ToLower(content)
+	for _, kw := range opts.Keywords {
+		kw = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(kw))
+		if kw != "" && strings.Contains(needle, kw) {
+			return true
+		}
+	}
+	return false
+}
+
+func (ch *Channel) buildCommentContent(data MessagingData) string {
+	body := buildMessageContent(data)
+	if !ch.config.CommentReplyOptions.IncludePostContext || data.PostID == "" || ch.postFetcher == nil {
+		return body
+	}
+
+	post, err := ch.postFetcher.GetPost(ch.stopCtx, data.PostID)
+	if err != nil {
+		slog.Debug("pancake: fetch post context failed", "post_id", data.PostID, "err", err)
+		return body
+	}
+	text := strings.TrimSpace(postText(post))
+	if text == "" {
+		return body
+	}
+	return "[Bài đăng] " + stripHTML(text) + "\n\n[Comment mới] " + body
+}

+func (ch *Channel) sendCommentReply(ctx context.Context, conversationID string, msg bus.OutboundMessage) error {
+	text := FormatOutbound(msg.Content, ch.platform)
+	if text == "" {
+		return nil
+	}
+
+	parts := splitMessage(text, ch.maxMessageLength())
+	for _, part := range parts {
+		ch.rememberOutboundEcho(conversationID, part)
+	}
+	for i, part := range parts {
+		if err := ch.apiClient.ReplyComment(ctx, conversationID, part); err != nil {
+			ch.handleAPIError(err)
+			for _, unsent := range parts[i:] {
+				ch.forgetOutboundEcho(conversationID, unsent)
+			}
+			return err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if ch.config.Features.FirstInbox {
+		senderID := ""
+		if msg.Metadata != nil {
+			senderID = msg.Metadata["sender_id"]
+		}
+		if senderID != "" {
+			ch.sendFirstInbox(ctx, conversationID, senderID)
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// sendFirstInbox sends a one-time private reply after a comment reply (best-effort).
+func (ch *Channel) sendFirstInbox(ctx context.Context, conversationID, senderID string) {
+	if _, alreadySent := ch.firstInboxSent.LoadOrStore(senderID, struct{}{}); alreadySent {
+		return
+	}
+	message := ch.config.FirstInboxMessage
+	if message == "" {
+		message = "Cảm ơn bạn đã comment! Mình có thể hỗ trợ thêm qua tin nhắn riêng."
+	}
+	if err := ch.apiClient.PrivateReply(ctx, conversationID, message); err != nil {
+		slog.Warn("pancake: first inbox send failed", "sender_id", senderID, "conversation_id", conversationID, "err", err)
+		ch.firstInboxSent.Delete(senderID) // allow retry on next comment
+	}
+}

new file mode 100644
index 0000000..af1045f

+package pancake
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"sync"
+	"time"
+
+	"golang.org/x/sync/singleflight"
+)
+
+const defaultPostCacheTTL = 15 * time.Minute
+
+type postCacheEntry struct {
+	posts     []PostInfo
+	expiresAt time.Time
+}
+
+// PostFetcher fetches and caches Pancake page posts. Pancake exposes posts as a
+// page-level collection, so singleflight uses a single "posts" key instead of a
+// per-postID key to avoid stampedes when many comments arrive concurrently.
+type PostFetcher struct {
+	apiClient *APIClient
+	cacheTTL  time.Duration
+	cache     sync.Map
+	sfGroup   singleflight.Group
+}
+
+// NewPostFetcher creates a PostFetcher with the given cache TTL string (e.g. "15m").
+func NewPostFetcher(client *APIClient, cacheTTLStr string) *PostFetcher {
+	ttl := defaultPostCacheTTL
+	if cacheTTLStr != "" {
+		if d, err := time.ParseDuration(cacheTTLStr); err == nil && d > 0 {
+			ttl = d
+		}
+	}
+	return &PostFetcher{apiClient: client, cacheTTL: ttl}
+}
+
+// GetPost returns the post for postID, using a TTL cache of the page's posts list.
+func (pf *PostFetcher) GetPost(ctx context.Context, postID string) (*PostInfo, error) {
+	if postID == "" || pf == nil || pf.apiClient == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+
+	posts, err := pf.getPosts(ctx)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	for i := range posts {
+		if posts[i].ID == postID {
+			return &posts[i], nil
+		}
+	}
+	return nil, nil
+}
+
+func (pf *PostFetcher) getPosts(ctx context.Context) ([]PostInfo, error) {
+	const key = "posts"
+	if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+		entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+		if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+			return entry.posts, nil
+		}
+		pf.cache.Delete(key)
+	}
+
+	val, err, _ := pf.sfGroup.Do(key, func() (any, error) {
+		if v, ok := pf.cache.Load(key); ok {
+			entry := v.(*postCacheEntry)
+			if time.Now().Before(entry.expiresAt) {
+				return entry.posts, nil
+			}
+		}
+		posts, err := pf.apiClient.ListPosts(ctx)
+		if err != nil {
+			return nil, err
+		}
+		pf.cache.Store(key, &postCacheEntry{
+			posts:     posts,
+			expiresAt: time.Now().Add(pf.cacheTTL),
+		})
+		return posts, nil
+	})
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, err
+	}
+	if val == nil {
+		return nil, nil
+	}
+	return val.([]PostInfo), nil
+}
+
+func postText(post *PostInfo) string {
+	if post == nil {
+		return ""
+	}
+	switch {
+	case post.Message != "":
+		return post.Message
+	case post.Content != "":
+		return post.Content
+	case post.Caption != "":
+		return post.Caption
+	case post.Description != "":
+		return post.Description
+	default:
+		return post.OriginalMessage
+	}
+}
